Britain and France Mediate the Spanish Civil War; Germany, Italy, and Portugal's Replies are Unclear; They Hope Other Countries Can Provide Supplementary Explanations; Spanish Rebels Oppose Mediation

(London) Regarding the proposal by the British and French governments to mediate the Spanish Civil War, the replies from Germany and Portugal were delivered to the British Foreign Office yesterday. After reviewing them, the Foreign Office believes that the content is still unclear and hopes that the governments of those countries can provide supplementary explanations. It is learned that the German government plans to issue a statement today to clearly explain its intentions, and it is hoped that the Portuguese government will also clearly state its attitude. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Paris) Regarding the proposal by Britain and France to mediate the Spanish Civil War, the German government has sent a reply to the British and French ambassadors in Berlin, stating that Germany is prepared to support all plans to restore peace in Spain and prevent the war from spreading to other parts of Europe. If other governments can propose concrete mediation measures, Germany is prepared to cooperate and study them. However, the German government regrets that other governments have not effectively agreed to Germany's wish to prevent the influx of volunteer soldiers into Spain. Germany believes that stopping direct and indirect interference must be dealt with as one issue. As for the German government's recognition of the Spanish Nationalist government, it is because it considers that no other elements in Spain can help its people to govern themselves due to the barbarous actions on the other side of the conflict. Therefore, it is difficult for Germany to reach any understanding with the Spanish government. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

(Berlin) The British and French governments recently sent notes to the governments of Germany, Italy, Portugal, and Russia, suggesting that they jointly find ways to mediate the Spanish Civil War. The German government yesterday sent separate notes to the British and French governments in response. It is learned that the content of the German note is divided into the following points:

(1) Germany is prepared to support all measures aimed at preventing the continued expansion of the Spanish Civil War.

(2) On August 27, the German government advised all countries to include the prohibition of volunteer soldiers going to Spain in the non-intervention measures. Unfortunately, other governments did not make a decision on this, which made the Spanish situation more serious. The German government now believes that measures to prohibit any direct or indirect interference in the Spanish Civil War should be discussed as a whole.

(3) Germany expresses sympathy for the cooperation of various countries in mediating the Spanish Civil War. However, at the same time, the German government has something to declare: the German government has previously recognized the Nationalist authorities as the legitimate government of Spain. This action expresses Germany's opinion that the government of Burgos is the only factor representing the Spanish people. Whether it is helpful to seek reconciliation with the opposition is questionable, because the opposition to the Nationalist government is now controlled by anarchists. Under these circumstances, the German government does not see the possibility of organizing a referendum for the Spanish people in accordance with normal procedures. However, if other governments can propose practical and concrete suggestions for mediating the civil war, the German government is still willing to consider its implementation. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(Rome) Regarding the proposal by the British and French governments to mediate the Spanish Civil War, the Italian government's reply was delivered to Britain yesterday. Its content is divided into three points:

(1) The Italian government shares the same feeling with the British and French governments, who both want to prevent the expansion of the Spanish civil unrest and hope that Spain will restore order.

(2) Regarding the issuance of a formal declaration, reiterating the various non-intervention measures and enriching them, the Italian government proposed at the beginning of the outbreak of the two countries' civil war that if the non-intervention policy is to be effective, then the recruitment of volunteer soldiers, the solicitation of subsidies, and various propaganda methods should all be prohibited. It is firmly believed that if this proposal had been implemented at that time, it would have been easier than now. Although the Italian government is still willing to join the United Kingdom in studying various measures to enrich the non-intervention agreement and strictly implement the monitoring system, it is "on the condition that all these measures are accepted."

(3) Regarding the proposal by the British and French governments to mediate the Spanish Civil War and order the people of that country to hold a referendum to determine the political system, Italy is also willing to accept it, but "the Italian government has doubts as to whether a referendum can be implemented in Spain under the current situation." Furthermore, from an objective point of view, "the Spanish Nationalist government has successively gained the support of the majority of the people and possesses a large part of the country's territory. The will of the Spanish people has already been expressed because of this, and it is undeniable." On the contrary, the Valencia government in that country has anarchistic tendencies, and its brutal acts are countless. "Therefore, reconciliation is extremely difficult. However, the Italian government is still willing to do its best to work for peace. If the governments of various countries believe that it is necessary to put forward various suggestions, Italy is naturally prepared to consider them in a spirit of friendly cooperation." (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Geneva) According to people from the Portuguese delegation to the League of Nations, the Portuguese government's reply to the proposal by Britain and France to mediate the Spanish Civil War expresses acceptance of the principle of implementing non-intervention measures. However, it does not recognize the possibility of mediation under the current circumstances. Portugal can only consider the practical methods of implementing mediation if both parties in the Spanish Civil War first accept mediation. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Salamanca: A key figure in the Nationalist government recently commented on the proposal by the British and French governments to mediate the civil war, saying, "The struggle waged by the Nationalist army has no room for reconciliation. If we want to end the struggle, it will be either our army winning or the Red Army surrendering. There is no other way. Those who propose mediation have not taken into account the true situation in Spain, and they are also ignorant of the root of the Spanish incident. In fact, the two concepts of religion and patriotism dominate the Spanish Civil War and do not allow for any concessions. Some say that the Spanish Civil War may affect the current situation in Europe. This statement is not without reason, but our goal is to rebuild a Catholic and imperial Spain, so we should not make any compromises." (Havas dispatch, 14th)

League of Nations Committee Discusses Amendment of the Covenant; Chilean Representative and Spanish Foreign Minister Negotiate the Issue of Relieving Women, Children, the Elderly, and the Weak

(Geneva) The Committee on the Amendment of the Covenant of the League of Nations, namely the Committee of Twenty-Eight, is scheduled to hold its first resolution meeting at 3:30 PM today in order to elect the Presidium and formulate the work program. It is generally believed that the Belgian representative, Mr. Bourquin, will come forward to serve as chairman. The work of the committee may have to be extended until the end of this week before it can be concluded. The French Permanent Representative to the League of Nations, former French Foreign Minister Mr. Peng Gu, arrived here at 9:40 AM today to participate in the meeting. Although Italy is one of the member states of the committee, it did not send personnel to attend. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Geneva) Regarding the Spanish Civil War issue, the Chairman of the Council of the League of Nations, the Chilean Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Mr. Edward, has agreed with the Spanish Minister of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Talier, to move a part of the Spanish refugees, especially women, children, the elderly, and the weak, housed in the Chilean Embassy in Madrid to a completely neutral area. After the temporary meeting of the Council of the League of Nations closes, Mr. Edward will continue the talks through diplomatic channels. He is scheduled to return to his post in London tomorrow evening. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Turkey Advocates Granting Autonomy to Ethnic Minorities in Syria

(Geneva) The temporary meeting of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to hold a closed meeting at 5 PM and then immediately hold an open meeting. The Committee on the Amendment of the Covenant of the League of Nations is scheduled to hold a meeting at 3:30 PM today. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Geneva) Regarding the issue of the Turkish ethnic minorities in the two cities of Alexandretta and Antioch in Syria, the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to discuss it this afternoon. The French and Turkish delegations were preparing separately this morning. According to the scheduled procedure, the Council will hold a closed meeting at 5 PM this afternoon, and then hold an open meeting, where Turkish Foreign Minister Mr. Rüştü will deliver a speech to explain his country's views. The French representative, French Foreign Minister Mr. Weygand, may submit a reply tomorrow morning. Mr. Weygand met this morning with British Undersecretary of State Lord Cranborne, Soviet Ambassador to France Mr. Potemkin, and Chairman of the Council of the League of Nations, the Chilean Ambassador to the United Kingdom, Mr. Edward. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

(Geneva) It is generally believed that Turkey will demand that each of these cities enjoy autonomy and be governed by the League of Nations, so that they are in the same position as the Free City of Danzig. From now until then, the Council will take several measures as a transition. It is generally believed that France and Turkey have always had strong diplomatic relations and want to maintain them. There will naturally be no difficulties when the Council discusses this case today. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Angora: The Turkish Prime Minister declared today that the Turkish government will demand independence for the ethnic minorities in Alexandretta. Madrid is Heavily Defended; French Newspaper Reporter Dies in a Plane Crash

Madrid: No battles took place in the vicinity of the city today. In addition, the weather was sunny, and many members of the militia took the opportunity to stroll around the city and take a break. There are often photographers on the streets taking pictures of militia and syndicalist figures. These people all take brave poses in front of the camera, holding weapons and pretending to shoot at invisible enemies, while young people watch from the side, laughing loudly. Until 4 PM, several cannon sounds were heard, and two shells fell near the telephone bureau, fortunately without injuring anyone. Mr. Trapol, a reporter for the French Paris Evening News, was shot by Nationalist planes while flying in the city of Pastrana (about 100 kilometers from Madrid) a few days ago, and eventually died of serious injuries. His remains have recently been transported from here to the port of Valencia in the southeast, and then transferred to France for burial. (Havas dispatch, 14th)

Madrid: Five government bombers and five fighter planes attacked the Vitoria airfield today, destroying it and shooting down two rebel bombers. One government plane also crashed. (National Telegram, 14th)

Talavanara: Special report from our correspondent: The government forces are heavily defended in the university district and the old royal palace area in the western suburbs of Madrid. Every night, at the sound of anything suspicious, they attack the Nationalist forces. The Moroccan guest army and regular army under their command do not return fire. The government forces have also placed strong barbed wire in front of the first trench on Rosales Avenue in the northwest suburbs, and used "chevaux de frise" to protect the forward patrols. On the northern side of the Dedune district, the government forces have built new fortifications with reinforced concrete. As for the southern side, the government forces' outpost seems to have retreated slightly. Observing the situation on the front lines of various countries, the government forces now seem to be preparing to resist the Nationalist forces' attack. The artillery teams of both sides did not move today, and only a few fighter planes flew in the air without dropping bombs. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Political Strife Resurfaces in Barcelona; Socialist Party Demands Reorganization of the Executive Yuan

Barcelona: Political strife has recently occurred within the Executive Yuan of the Catalonia Autonomous Region, and there is talk of reorganizing the Executive Yuan. A key figure in the Unified Socialist Party of Catalonia, Congressman Komo Lera, who once held an important position in the Executive Yuan, has issued a statement explaining the political strife, which is worthy of attention. He said: Since Germany and Italy recognized the Franco government, the political situation has changed. The Unified Socialist Party to which I belong was the first to raise this issue, because the current power of the autonomous region government to plan the war and resist the rebels is not sufficient. Therefore, our party proposes to reorganize the Executive Yuan of the autonomous region government into a government with full powers, so that the National Confederation of Labor (CNT) belonging to the anarchist faction, the General Union of Workers (UGT) belonging to the socialist faction, the Republican Left of Catalonia (ERC), the Metalworkers' Union, etc., can all participate, and the Intelligence Committee and the National Defense Department should be abolished, because all members of the Executive Yuan have full power to select and replace their colleagues. The reorganized Executive Yuan should devote all its efforts to directing the war, and the issue of the future social organization should be temporarily shelved. Komo Lera also confirmed the claim that the Unified Socialist Party demanded that the Marxist-Leninist Workers' Party (POUM) withdraw from the Executive Yuan, saying that the POUM attacked several decisions of the Executive Yuan, especially its criticism of the Soviet Union, so it could no longer be allowed to participate in the government. Finally, he clearly condemned the various tendencies to separate Catalonia from Spain, saying that "international fascists are spreading rumors" to mislead people into believing that the separation movement is supported by the Third International, which is completely untrue. According to Komo Lera, who is known to be friendly with Soviet Consul Endonov in Catalonia, this statement shows that the Soviet government is frankly opposed to Catalonia's independence. In addition, the Marxist-Leninist Workers' Party (POUM) newspaper "Combat" opposed the proposal of the Unified Socialist Party to abolish the Intelligence Committee and the National Defense Department, saying that these two agencies are necessary for the working class to monitor internal order and military organization and should not be abolished. "Combat" also opposed the proposal of the Unified Socialist Party to temporarily shelve the social revolution during the war. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

Inter-American Conference; Mexican Proposal

Buenos Aires, Argentina – Although the Inter-American Peace Conference did not convene today, the Mexican delegation still submitted a peace plan consisting of the following points:

(1) Adjusting the existing various peace treaties and consolidating them into one.

(2) Establishing an Inter-American Court.

(3) Not recognizing land acquired by force.

(4) Prohibiting the use of force to collect debts.

(5) Countries should agree on reciprocal trade agreements to give the Western Hemisphere priority over European and Asian countries.

(6) Prohibiting the supply of munitions and economic aid to aggressor nations.

This plan will be formally presented at the conference in Lima, Peru. Simultaneously, a neutrality treaty that has already been signed by the representatives of various countries will be submitted to the full assembly for a final vote on Tuesday. (Guomin dispatch, 13th)

Current Commentary

Finance and Prices in Extraordinary Times

— Liu

Yesterday, the disorder in the Shanghai commodity market and the sharp fluctuations in prices were a clear reflection of the extraordinary situation in the economic sphere. Government bonds are the most sensitive to the impact of the situation. Initially, there was a discussion about not opening the market at all. Once the market opened, all unified bonds fell by four yuan and reached the limit. This is an unprecedented phenomenon since the unified bonds were listed. Cotton yarn was even more peculiar. The current month's yarn opened down by more than five yuan, but immediately rebounded by twelve yuan in the second session. Cotton also rose by one yuan several jiao. Apart from the psychological effects of merchants, there is really not much reason for these rises and falls. What is most astonishing is that flour, wheat, grains, oil, and bean cakes are rising as if there is no end in sight. For example, flour prices for the January period and beyond are as high as four yuan and three jiao or more. Future wheat opened at seven yuan, one jiao and two fen, which is an unprecedented price in decades. Soybean oil is already at twenty-four yuan and four jiao per dan, and raw oil has also reached twenty-two yuan. If we recall last year's market conditions, just in terms of oil alone, our living expenses have more than doubled.

The margin of fluctuation has not changed much in the past year. Yesterday, due to speculative opportunities, there was a fluctuation of fourteen yuan in one day. The result was a rise of five yuan and four jiao. In addition, items such as metals and tung oil were suspended due to the unrest of the situation. In fact, extreme rises and falls are not right. Suspension of transactions is also unnecessary. Knowing that the situation is unstable, we should not alarm each other, thus adding to the factors of instability. Because if we want to achieve a favorable resolution to the current dangerous situation, we must also strive for economic stability.

The way to stabilize the economy is to first stabilize finance. In this extraordinary period, the people should no longer have any doubts about legal tender. The situation of everyone rushing to buy foreign exchange yesterday was very distressing. We should know that only by stabilizing finance can we extricate ourselves from the困境. Otherwise, pursuing individual interests will only lead to a harmful outcome for everyone. We believe that in this period, those who are fully responsible for finance should make thorough plans for finance. The general public, especially financial, industrial, and commercial circles, and the wealthy, should also absolutely trust the government's monetary policy for their own sake and for the sake of the country.

As for the soaring prices, which were so severe yesterday, it is clearly an abnormal state. If we do not seek to remedy the situation, the future is very worrying. We believe that those who are responsible for guiding industry and commerce should immediately come forward to correct unreasonable price increases. Sometimes, it may be necessary to stop them. Because passively restricting is the simplest way to maintain the market. Now that the closing period is approaching, if there is a change in the economic sphere, industry and commerce will inevitably suffer a major blow. We must take precautions before it happens.

No Prospect of Fisheries Agreement Between Japan and the Soviet Union; Various Parties Criticize Arita's Diplomatic Policy; Hirota Cabinet May Resign Next Spring

(Tokyo) It is extremely clear that there is no hope of signing a fisheries agreement between Japan and the Soviet Union before the end of this year, since the first meeting between Japanese Ambassador to the Soviet Union Shigemitsu Aoi and Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov. Litvinov stated that the Soviet government does not believe that the purpose of the Japanese-German agreement is solely to oppose communism, because the geographical location of Japan and Germany clearly indicates the goals of the two countries. Therefore, the Soviet government does not want to answer before deciding on its new attitude. The Soviet Union's tough stance can be seen from Litvinov's statement. Arita instructed Shigemitsu yesterday to redouble his efforts to urge the Soviet Union to sign, but the general public fears that this effort will be ineffective. Japanese newspapers are criticizing the diplomatic policies of Hirota and Arita more and more intensely. It is rumored that various parties are preparing to impeach the cabinet. At the same time, the Privy Council is also seriously investigating the government's responsibility for the failure of diplomacy. It is now feared that Arita's resignation is unavoidable, and the period is probably in early spring next year. (Central News Agency dispatch, 14th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the signing of the Japan-Soviet Fisheries Treaty, when Ambassador Shigemitsu met with Litvinov on the 9th, the Soviet Union replied that the Soviet government is now considering measures to sign the Japan-Soviet Fisheries Treaty, and will notify the Japanese government after a decision is made. Therefore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is waiting for a reply from the Soviet Union with optimistic observations. However, from the Soviet Union's perspective, the obligations under the treaty not only include the obligation to sign the fisheries treaty, but also the impact it has suffered since the treaty was abolished is significantly greater than that of Japan. Therefore, from the following points of view, it seems impossible to foresee that the Soviet Union will refuse to sign.

Japan's fishing rights are long-standing vested interests that have existed for two years, and have even been confirmed based on the Sakhalin-Chishima Exchange Treaty and the Japan-Russia Basic Treaty. Moreover, according to Article 11 of the Japan-Russia Peace Treaty, the Soviet Union has an obligation to conclude an agreement with Japan. Therefore, since the Soviet Union recognizes the existence of international treaties, the Soviet Union must not refuse to sign the fisheries treaty.

According to the provisions of the Fisheries Treaty, the Soviet Union created a format for employing Japanese citizens in North Pacific fisheries in order to maintain its national dignity. If it is in a state of no treaty, it is obvious that Japanese citizens will forcibly fish in the North Pacific. Therefore, the dignity of the Soviet Union will be flawed.

The Fisheries Treaty restricts the freedom of Japanese North Pacific fisheries and allows the exercise of fishing rights with certain restrictions. Therefore, if Japan is free from this restriction and freely fishes, the Soviet Union will be greatly disadvantaged, and Japan's fishing rights will have virtually no impact. The Soviet Union is disturbed by national debate until early spring next year, and this is not difficult to predict. Judging from the objective situation above, the ending will certainly be signed soon. (Daimon dispatch, 14th)

Former King of England Arrives in Vienna; Stays in an 800-Year-Old Castle

(Vienna) Former King Edward of England arrived today at Count Losos' 800-year-old castle, and immediately spoke with Mrs. Simpson by telephone for a long time. The former king's arrival in Austria this time is not comparable to a monarch's tour. He only brought one attendant and one dog. When he arrived in Vienna, only the British minister and some Austrian officials welcomed him. There was no lively scene of military music and troops around. (Guomin dispatch, 14th)

(Vienna) The Duke of Windsor, the former King of England, arrived here last night from Innsbruck in western Austria by special train. He looked very healthy and immediately took a car to Enzesfeld, fifteen miles outside Vienna, as a guest of Baron Rothschild. Enzesfeld is a very large hunting ground, occupying fifteen square miles, with a giant manor built in the middle, with forty rooms. When the former king's special train approached the station last night, the police immediately posted sentries in front of and behind the sleeping car, not allowing anyone to approach. When the car arrived at the station, the only greeters were Sir Selby, the British Minister to Austria, and no representatives from the Austrian government were at the station. The former king wore a black coat with a leather collar and a black and red wool scarf. After entering the station, he went back to the VIP lounge and then suddenly retreated, inviting photographers to take pictures of him. The group then returned to the platform, and the former king happily allowed the photographers to take his portrait. He then boarded Baron Rothschild's car. His cavalry officer, Lieutenant Colonel Lief, relayed to everyone that he had not decided how long to stay in Austria, and expressed his gratitude to the reporters and photographers who came with him for not disturbing him during the journey. The former king brought a small hunting dog on this trip, and the public only saw him twice during this trip. The first time was when he went for a walk at the port of Boulogne in northwestern France, and the second time was when the train arrived in Innsbruck, and the former king admired the snowy scenery outside the window. The former king's whereabouts are kept secret. The police in England, France, Austria, and Switzerland have all provided strict protection. The French Detective Department once hung a carriage behind the special train. Every time it arrived at a station, the detectives were distributed on the platform where the former king's sleeping car was parked. It is said that there were police guarding every kilometer along the way. When the train arrived in Basel, Switzerland, the French and Swiss police changed defenses. When the train arrived at Buchs, a town on the Austrian-Swiss border, the Austrian and Swiss police also changed defenses. The reporters traveling with the special train almost lost track of the former king. Later, in order to comfort the reporters, the former king finally agreed to tell them his final destination. (Reuters dispatch, 14th)

(Vienna) After staying in Enzesfeld for a few days, the former king will go to Kitzbühel for a short stay to engage in winter sports, and then visit Prince Paul of Yugoslavia, the regent. He will then return to Vienna to consult with ear specialist Dr. Neumann. The special train taken by the former king was attached to the Paris-Vienna express train in Zurich, Switzerland, and headed to Austria. At noon, it arrived in Feldkirch, a city on the border between Switzerland and Austria. More than 50 reporters flocked to the train to find the former king, but the former king was dining in the carriage and did not go out, so they did not get to see him. Later, when the special train arrived in Innsbruck, a postal and telecommunications bureau official boarded the train and presented the former king with a telegram from England, asking the former king to speak to London on the long-distance telephone immediately. However, the former king only replied with a telegram. When the special train arrived in Kitzbühel, the former king received another telegram. According to some people, the telegram was sent by Mrs. Simpson, who had taken a train to meet him in Vienna. However, other people claimed to have seen Mrs. Simpson in the former king's carriage. After reading the second telegram, the former king ordered his entourage to inform the reporters traveling with him that his trip was of a private nature and asked them not to disturb him. What he wanted to say had been explained in detail in his radio broadcast last Friday, and there was nothing to add. Once he arrived in Vienna, he would allow the reporters to take pictures of him. The special train stopped in Kitzbühel for a longer time than usual, because the manager of the "Grand Hotel" had to board the train to greet him. The former king received him and told him that he would return to Kitzbühel soon. (Havas dispatch, 13th)

(London) It was learned today that Parliament is willing to grant former King Edward a considerable retirement allowance. Members of Parliament believe that if the former king's financial situation is not very good, or if he places himself or the government and the royal family in an awkward situation, the people will always remember his eventful reign of eleven months. Therefore, the opinion of Parliament seems to be in favor of the government immediately allocating a retirement allowance of £50,000, and it is believed that although Edward did not fully satisfy the people after ascending the throne, he was the most outstanding Prince of Wales in British history when he was the heir apparent. At present, all parties seem to be doing their best to promote the idea of quickly forgetting the period when Edward was in power. The impression Edward gave people was very different from that of the late King George V. The new king's name, George VI, also has this intention. Newspapers today all praise the new king's sense of responsibility and his concern for the throne, and are full of praise for the new queen's demeanor. (Guomin dispatch, 13th)

U.S. Industrial Requisition Plan; Secretary of War Says There Is No Intention to Prepare for War; It Is Also of the Same Nature as the Neutrality Law

(Washington) The Associated Press learned today that more than 20,000 factories across the United States have been investigated in detail by the Army and Navy General Staffs in order to draft a wartime factory mobilization plan. The investigation items include the factory's capital, the number of workers, the items produced, and the quantity produced. Secretary of War Woodring said today, "Now we know what is needed in wartime, and the location and time required for the production of all supplies." Woodring also solemnly declared that the industrial requisition plan drafted by him and Secretary of the Navy Swanson had no intention of preparing for war, but only wanted to enable the U.S. military to use domestic resources during wartime to obtain supplies in the most economical and effective way. This plan, even if implemented, is of the same nature as the Neutrality Law and will not take effect until after a declaration of war. However, once a declaration of war is made, the president will have full power to control all domestic finance, transportation, agriculture, industry, and mining. As for the content of the plan, it includes the following points: (1) Stipulate prices, wages, land prices, and rents. (2) Control the manufacture and distribution of goods with a license system. (3) Strictly manage the nation's commodity, stock, and securities trading markets. (4) Prevent hoarding and speculation. (5) Requisition industrial management talents to serve the government. (6) Requisition all industries. (Guomin dispatch, 13th)

The Momentum of the Puppet Troops in Northern Chahar Has Faded Away, While the Bandit Troops in Jehol Have Become More Active. The Majority of the Bandit Troops are Concentrating in Guyuan and Advancing Westward Step by Step. A Certain Party is Transporting Large Quantities of Military Supplies to Aid the Puppet Troops in Jehol.

Jia Temple Dispatch: The puppet bandit troops of Li Shou-hsin and Wang Ying in Northern Chahar, after their recent failed counterattacks on Bailingmiao, Northern Sui, and Wuchuan, have become increasingly disorganized. After the successive defections of Jin Xianzhang and Shi Yushan from Wang's troops, they have already disintegrated. The remaining troops of Li Shou-hsin are also dwindling. On October 10, a certain special agency here, after discovering that Wang Ying himself was indeed in contact with the Sui army to express his allegiance, was extremely angry. It immediately notified all special agencies in Northern Chahar to offer a large reward for Wang Ying's capture. The reason is that Wang Ying has been active in foreign affairs since the autumn of this year, for more than four months, and has spent more than one million yuan in military expenses. This decisive battle was launched, and new-style weapons were exchanged with his troops. Now, nothing has been achieved, and his troops have turned over all their sharp weapons to the Sui army. Therefore, they hate him to the bone. If he is captured, he will follow in the footsteps of Dao Yi, which is Wang Ying's fate. Few people know the whereabouts of Wang himself. As for the current situation in Northern Chahar, I will briefly describe what I have seen and heard as follows:

The Jehol Army: Suddenly Active

Since the puppet bandits in Northern Chahar suffered several defeats, their momentum has faded away. A certain party took this opportunity to order its regular troops and the bandit troops in Jehol to advance westward step by step, replacing the puppet bandits in their former positions. Therefore, the Jehol army has been actively deployed recently. Wang Jingshou's troops are responsible for the defense of the Duolun, Zhangbei, and Nanhouchang areas. Zhang Hai-peng is responsible for the defense of Guyuan, Kangbao Baochang, and Shangdu. Their regular troops are interspersed among them. The majority of the Jehol army is now concentrating in Zhanyuan, gradually advancing westward. Today (November 11), the head of a certain special agency declared to the bandits and puppets here that they will never be allowed to retreat another step. It has been decided to set up a forward supply station in Zhangbei, and the main supply station will still be located in Duolun. It is also heard that a certain party intends to dig trenches along the Great Wall, which is currently under planning, probably as a precaution when necessary.

Recent Deployment of the Jehol Army

The current deployment of the Jehol army is as follows: More than 1,000 artillerymen of Zhang Hai-peng's rebel army, carrying more than 30 steel cannons, arrived at the Li Jiayingzi in Baochang County on the evening of the 9th of this month. Eight hundred cavalrymen arrived at Yutiaogou. In Tuchenzi, which belongs to Kangbao County, there are also more than 800 infantrymen of the same troops and 300 regular troops of a certain party. More than 3,000 people have been concentrated between Shangdu and Jia Temple. There are also 2,000 troops in Pangjiang. Wang Jingshou's troops are advancing from Duolun to Houchang. About 1,000 regular troops of a certain party are stationed in Qitai and Batai west of Shangdu and Pangjiang. The security team they recruited is now stationed in Daolanhada and Shitai, west of Shangdu, after the failed counterattack on Bailingmiao. In addition, there are more than 3,000 Mongolian bandit troops stationed in the Hatuoha area west of Shangdu. The majority of Li Shou-hsin's rebels are now stationed in Shangdu. Li himself often travels between Jia Temple and Shangdu.

A Certain Party is Transporting Weapons to Help the Bandits

The weapons and ammunition used by the bandits and puppet troops in Northern Chahar are fully supplied by a certain party. The large shipment of ammunition transported from Tianjin the other day has been completely transported to Zhangbei, Jia Temple, Shangdu, and Nanhouchang. Most of the poison gas shells were transported to Nanhouchang to prepare for a second westward invasion and reconciliation, using aircraft and poison gas as the main weapons. The technical personnel who guide the release of poison gas arrived in Zhangbei on the evening of the 9th of this month, about a dozen people. The aircraft pilots arrived in Duolun from Chifeng on the 7th of this month, about thirty people. Today (November 11), they arrived in Zhangbei and transferred to the Nanhouchang Pass. The routes for a certain party to supply military supplies to the rebel troops are very convenient, one via the Ping-Sui Railway and the other via Jehol, greatly aiding the bandits.

Han Fu-qu's Proclamation: Taking Safeguarding the Country and Protecting the People as His Mission - Those Who Create Rumors and Stir Up Trouble Will Be Severely Punished

Jinan Dispatch: Han Fu-qu, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government and Commander of the Shandong Security Force, in view of the recent unclear situation and the deepening national crisis, and for the sake of local security, has issued a proclamation strictly prohibiting the creation of rumors and incidents. The full text of the proclamation reads: "For the proclamation, recently the situation has been unstable, the national crisis is deepening, and those who like to cause trouble and rejoice in misfortune often make reckless speculations, causing disturbances and doubts, which are not conducive to local security. This Chairman and Commander has always taken safeguarding the country and protecting the people as his mission, and cannot but take precautions in advance. From now on, anyone who creates rumors and stirs up trouble sufficient to disturb the people's hearts will be dealt with by military law once discovered. In addition to ordering the military and police to investigate and arrest them at any time, this proclamation is issued for public knowledge. All people from all walks of life must strictly abide by it and not violate it. This proclamation is hereby issued, Han, Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government and Commander of the Shandong Provincial Security Force." (13th)

Recent Financial Situation in Guangdong Province: The Authorities are Actively Purchasing Silver from Various Subordinate Areas; The Conversion to the Silver Dollar Standard is Not Yet Possible in the Short Term; The Business Community Again Requests a Reduction in the Additional 5% Rate

Guangzhou Dispatch: Since the authorities actively reorganized Guangdong's finances, considerable progress has been made in purchasing silver. Therefore, there has recently been an increase in the issuance of Guangdong mill notes to facilitate the purchase of silver. The reason why villagers in various subordinate areas are selling silver one after another is that the end of the year is approaching, the rural economy is difficult, and they have no choice but to exchange their daily savings for general mill notes to maintain the status quo. It is estimated that there are still about 10 million yuan worth of silver in various subordinate areas. Currently, the authorities are using mill notes to collect silver, so there is no talk of converting to the silver dollar standard yet. However, the ratio between the silver dollar (national currency) and mill notes has remained between an additional 5% (or an additional 4.9% and some change) for several days. Most merchants believe that this is ultimately not a blessing for the people of Guangdong, because Guangdong mill notes have considerable value and cannot be depreciated so much. People in the business community have repeatedly requested the authorities to change this ratio between silver dollars and Guangdong mill notes to avoid huge losses to merchants, but the financial authorities have not responded. The 5% ratio is determined by the central government based on various circumstances and is difficult to change rashly. Therefore, the Guangzhou Industrial Federation has recently submitted another request to reduce the rate. The petition is as follows: "We have found that Guangdong Province has always used mill dollars as the standard for paying national taxes. Before 1932, an additional 2% or 2.5% was added for water compensation. Before the recovery and in the early years of the Republic of China, the ratio for silver dollars was an additional 1.5%. Recently, in August of this year, it was set at an additional 3%. When the Guangdong situation was unified, politics were clarified, and a new beginning was made with the people, the central government remembered the sufferings of the people of Guangdong over the years under cruel governance and heavy burdens, and resolutely banned opium and gambling, abolished harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies, and relieved the people of Guangdong from suffering. Suddenly, the ratio for silver dollars was raised to an additional 5%. The harm to the people has not yet been thoroughly eliminated, and the burden of higher water compensation has been abruptly increased, which is not worth the loss. How can the people's lives bear it? Guangdong Province has suffered the impact of the world's economic downturn for years, and all industries have declined. If we add the high water compensation for exchanging mill notes for silver dollars, then the mill notes issued and circulated in the market by the two banks of the province and city amount to more than 100 million yuan. Discounting by an additional 5%, only about 80 million silver dollars can be obtained, which is invisibly one-third less. The entire economy of Guangdong is tantamount to bankruptcy. How can we hope for its recovery? It is more than enough to maintain it in many ways, but one end is destroyed and there is more than enough. The provincial business community has discussed it repeatedly in recent days, and unanimously decided that the ratio of mill notes to silver dollars should be set at an additional 3% for water compensation, which is indeed appropriate. Judging from the public opinion of all sectors, it is also the same. The entire membership of our association has further studied it and believes that the economic life and death of Guangdong Province is at a critical juncture, and the gains and losses are of great importance. Moreover, exchanging mill notes for silver dollars is nothing more than exchanging notes for notes. Even if it is exchanged at the same price, the central government's finances will not suffer any losses, while the economy of the people of Guangdong will regain a slightly higher position. If it can be balanced with foreign exchange in the future, then all industries will be easier to maintain, and vitality can be gradually restored. We are grateful to the central government for its kindness, and the people of Guangdong have made a contribution equal to rebuilding. We earnestly request the government officials to give special consideration, listen to the public opinion of the entire province, and issue a clear order that Guangdong Province's mill notes be allowed to follow the ratio of an additional 3% for silver dollars, so as to reassure the people and maintain the Guangdong situation. The Guangzhou Industrial Federation, all members, respectfully bow." (December 12)

Huainan Railway Expands Joint Transportation; Huai River Shipping Increases Schedules; Railway Expands Joint Transportation Stations

Bengbu Dispatch: Since the Huainan Railway launched the Huai River joint transportation, water and land transportation has been quite convenient, and business is booming. The Huai River Shipping Cooperative, which handles joint transportation here, initially only used the Feipeng and Feiying steamboats to operate the short Beng-Tian route, traveling between Bengbu and Tianjia'an. Later, as passenger and cargo increased and ships were insufficient, they purchased a Lishang small wheel and leased a Hui Xing diesel boat from Hui Tong Company, successively joining the route. Before long, the Huaijia, Jianghuai, Yingshang, and Tai'an four small wheels of Changzhun Company also joined the cooperative. At this point, the joint transportation office had eight ships, operating on a rotating schedule. Last month, the Beng-Zheng long route was added, with two express boats traveling between Bengbu and Zhengyang, respectively. Recently, the Beng-Huai short route has been added, with four upbound and downbound ships operating daily between Bengbu and Huaiyuan, to facilitate merchants and travelers. It was test-sailed yesterday (11th) and the results were good. And the goods near the cooperative wharf are piled up like mountains. The company recently set up a freight station to facilitate the stacking of goods. The Huainan Railway, in order to facilitate merchants and promote joint transportation, has been approved by the Shanghai-Nanjing, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, and Jiangnan Railways to handle the joint transportation of ordinary goods in addition to joint transportation for goods such as rice, wheat, and soybeans. All cargo names and full or partial carloads are not restricted. The two railways have also opened up freight originating on the Huainan Railway, and the joint transportation stations have been expanded, adding various wharfs along the Huai River that belong to the Huai River Shipping Cooperative as joint transportation stations. They have already jointly revised the interim measures for the three-railway cargo joint transportation and submitted them to the Ministry of Railways for instructions. It has been temporarily approved to follow and implement expansion.

Zhejiang Province: Bumper Cotton Harvest This Year; Cotton Fields Exceed 560,000 Mu; Output Exceeds 240,000 Dan

Quzhou Dispatch: Zhejiang Province has always been known as a region with abundant cotton production in the southeast. In recent years, the provincial authorities have actively implemented production and construction, and have made efforts to promote cotton planting. The improved cotton fields in various counties have increased from several thousand mu to more than 100,000 mu, and the production of upland cotton has increased from several thousand dan to more than 100,000 dan. The increase in rural income has been estimated at more than one million yuan. This year, the promotion of cotton fields in various counties has reached more than 100,000 mu, including 50,000 mu planted with Million China Cotton in the implementation areas of Hangzhou, Xiaoshan, and Yuyao, and 60,000 mu planted with acclimatized American cotton in the implementation areas of Haiyan, Shangyu, Cixi, Zhenhai, and Dinghai. This year, due to suitable weather, even rainfall, and the guidance of promotion personnel, sowing, fertilization, weeding, and pest control were carried out in accordance with the predetermined procedures. Cotton farmers in various places have been willing to accept it because they have sold at good prices for many years. Therefore, the bumper harvest of improved cotton this year is unprecedented. The Million China Cotton in the Xiaoshan implementation area and the acclimatized American cotton in Nanhong Village and Meishan Island in the Zhenhai implementation area are considered the best. The yield of Million China Cotton is more than 150 catties per mu, and the yield of acclimatized American cotton is more than 200 catties per mu, with some reaching 300 catties. The yields in the Haiyan and Yuyao implementation areas are also good. In total, among the more than 20 counties that produce cotton in the province, the largest producer is Yuyao, with 15,000 mu of improved cotton fields, producing 11,520 dan, and 745,762 mu of native cotton fields, producing 563,796 dan. The total area of native cotton and improved cotton is 760,763 mu, and the total output is 575,316 dan. Second is Xiaoshan, with 16,000 mu of improved cotton fields, producing 61,440 dan, and 246,005 mu of native cotton fields, producing 88,560 dan. The total area is 262,000 mu and the output is 94,704 dan. Third is Pinghu, with 1,200 mu of improved cotton fields, producing 641 dan, and 138,800 mu of native cotton fields, producing 49,963 dan. The total area is 140,000 mu and the output is 50,429 dan. The remaining 10+ counties, including Cixi, have a total of 63,200 mu of improved cotton fields, producing 34,147 dan, and a total of 496,091 mu of native cotton fields, producing 198,070 dan. The total area of cotton fields in each county is 561,285 mu, and the total output is 244,212 dan. The average yield per mu is 180 catties of improved seed cotton and 137 catties of native seed cotton. According to the market price last month, each mu can earn 29 yuan, 5 jiao, and 3 fen of silver, and each mu of native cotton can earn 20 yuan, 6 jiao, and 4 fen of silver. The income from one mu of improved cotton is on average about 9 yuan higher than that of native cotton. If we consider the recent soaring price of cotton yarn, the estimated value will still be more than this amount. (December 11)

Robberies Occur One After Another in Songjiang Punan

At 10:00 PM on the 8th, the home of Wu Youquan, a farmer from the 11th Jia, 3rd Bao, of Jinshan Mouth Town, Punan, was robbed by more than 20 thieves, each holding two long and short guns, who broke into the house and ransacked the bedroom, robbing 23 silver dollars and clothes, etc., and fled northeast. At 2:00 AM the next morning, another robbery occurred in the same area, in Yinglong Township, in the homes of farmers Zhou Muchang, Zhou Tongsheng, and Zhou Xiaogen from the 2nd Jia, 5th Bao of the 9th Tu. More than 10 thieves also committed the robbery, carrying away 160 catties of harvested cotton and five pieces of homespun cloth on Zhou Muchang's small boat and fleeing. The incident has been reported to the Ninth Resident Office for investigation. It is feared that it was committed by the same gang, it is said.

Suzhou Zhang Xiaoshi Painting Exhibition

Zhang Xiaoshi, a famous painter from Songjiang, previously traveled north to the old capital, making great efforts in painting, and his art has become more refined. He arrived in Suzhou yesterday and exhibited hundreds of his recent works, holding an exhibition for seven days at Chongzhen Palace inside the Banmen, from the 14th to the 30th. His brother, Zishi, also has several recent works participating. It is heard that a few percent of the proceeds from the sale of paintings will be donated to comfort the soldiers guarding the territory in Suiyuan, fulfilling the duties of a citizen.

All Circles Denounce Zhang Xueliang

Zhang Xueliang of Xi'an led his troops to betray the country and kidnapped the leader. When the news spread, all circles in Wu and Ma were shocked. Commander Song of the 36th Division stationed in Suzhou and Special Commissioner Sun of Deng County convened representatives from all circles at 10:00 AM on the 14th at the Zhongshan Hall for an emergency meeting to discuss measures. It was unanimously resolved to jointly telegraph the central government, requesting a clear order to punish Zhang Xueliang, and to send a telegram nationwide, asking for unanimous denouncement of Zhang. It was also decided to telegraph Zhang Xueliang to swiftly restore Chiang Kai-shek's freedom, and to telegraph Chairman Fu of Suiyuan, requesting him to continue to work hard to suppress bandits and puppets. Wu Huishan and Fan Junbo were recommended to draft and send the above telegrams. The Xin Su Club also decided to denounce and punish Zhang Xueliang, and other groups also expressed their views. The County Party Headquarters convened an emergency meeting of all county party members at 4:00 PM on the 14th to discuss the issue of punishing the rebels.

Suzhou City Under Special Alert

Zhang Hanqi, Director of the Public Security Bureau, in view of the rampant theft and robbery during the winter defense period, which is a serious threat to the local area, in order to maintain local security, ordered a special alert throughout the city starting at 10:00 PM on the 13th. Pedestrians were checked at all key points, and additional patrol teams were dispatched throughout the night to prevent the activities of petty thieves. At the same time, orders were issued to subordinates that no leave would be allowed during the winter defense period. The military and police joint inspection office also sent teams to patrol, and all recreational venues and night venues closed early.

Taicang: Banditry Rises Again in the Four Townships

As winter arrives, banditry is rampant again in the four townships. The Su Township Head of Yiqiao Township in the county's third district and four families of villagers surnamed Ji, Pu, and Gu each received two threatening letters from bandits delivered by post, demanding 10,000 yuan in funds, with intense wording. Zhu's Hotel in the Pailou market also received the same threatening letter. The recipients have reported the matter to the county for investigation. In addition, Sun Guilin, a Chen's accounting office employee, was returning to the city after collecting rent when three people suddenly appeared on the Xihu Road near the South Gate Station. Speaking with a Hakka accent, they blocked his way and robbed all the more than 20 yuan in rent he had collected. He immediately reported to the Public Security Bureau requesting an investigation.

Wuxi: Rice Market Suddenly Falls

Since the rice industry market in this county learned of Zhang Xueliang's sudden rebellion in Xi'an, the market situation suddenly softened, and transactions gradually became scarce. The price of rice such as coarse rice and white rice has fallen by about 5 jiao per dan, and the price of rice such as japonica rice and indica rice has fallen by more than 2 jiao. Wheat has also fallen by about 2 jiao. Merchants from Xi'an who had ordered rice and grain in Wuxi had shipped 7,000 to 8,000 shi in the past two days, and there are still more than 20,000 shi of rice and grain piled up at the station, waiting to be loaded and shipped.

Women's Team Set Off to Promote

The Publicity Department of the local Women's Association held its first meeting at the County Party Headquarters yesterday. The chairman, Cai Xiangyun, resolved: 1. To organize a fundraising team, recommending Wang Huilan, Zhou Xuan, Cai Xiangyun, Zhu Wenying, Sun Manshi, Xu Jingxia, Zhou Wanru, Yao Huizhen, and Sun De as the team leaders. 2. To set the publicity date for 1:00 PM on the 20th of this month. 6. Changzhou: Confiscated Export Rice

Since the Jiangsu Provincial Government complied with the Executive Yuan's order to lift the ban on rice exports, according to the Zhenhai Customs investigation, the number of rice shipments transported by ships and lighters has reached more than 5,000 shi in recent days. Merchants are hoarding and speculating, and rice prices are soaring everywhere. Zhang Mingfu, the manager of the Hengtai Rice Store in Xutang Town in the fourth district of Wuyi, hired a boat the night before last to load more than 100 shi of rice, but it is unknown where it was being transported. Chen Zhesheng, the director of the ship inspection office in the town, sent someone to investigate. Since there was no transportation passport and no sales location, it was immediately detained. On one hand, the security team stationed in the town was guarding it, and on the other hand, Director Chen reported to Wang Zushu, the district chief of the fourth district, who telegraphed the county government for verification. The county government then telegraphed the provincial government for instructions on how to deal with it.

Changshu: Confiscated Smuggled Rice

It is recently learned that a certain party is buying a large amount of grain, so all parties are paying close attention to the transportation of food at various ports. Ten days ago, the Xunpu port here was intercepted by the patrol ship of the town office and seized two rice boats carrying more than 90 shi of rice. There was no rice transportation passport. Shen Chuan's Xia Donglin claimed to have been entrusted by Chongming rice merchant Ni Shengmao to come to Changshu to purchase rice. After being investigated by the county government, it was confirmed that it was smuggled out of the country. It has now been reported to the provincial government for approval. In accordance with the measures prohibiting rice exports, all of it will be confiscated and turned over to the public, and 40% will be used as a reward for those who handled the case. The county government is now recruiting merchants to auction it off, which can fetch about 600 yuan. It is also reported that the Baimao port security detachment also seized a smuggled rice boat and will handle it in the same way.

Yangzhou: Water Patrol Team Seizes Opium

The provincial capital's water patrol team, based on reports that a large amount of opium was being transported to the Bagang port for sale, dispatched multiple detectives and other personnel, traveling by boat to the port on the 7th. They seized 45 bags of opium at the Datong Wheel Branch dock, and then arrested the branch manager Yan Zhenglu, the opium offender Yan Hanzhang, and a Mr. Zhang from the Hongda Tea House, and transferred them to the province for disposal.

Bengbu: Unrest in the Lower Reaches of the Changhuai River

The Hongze Lake area in the lower reaches of the Changhuai River has always been a breeding ground for bandits. In this year of famine, the *Huanfu* are restless, and the bandits are lurking and multiplying. Recently, scattered bandits have been discovered near Shuanggou, taking the opportunity to rob and loot. Chen Shaowu Hotel in the town was recently robbed clean, and the owner was stabbed and a child was kidnapped. Yang Zehuan, the director of the Wuhe Water Police Bureau, sent a team to suppress the bandits, killing the hostage and capturing the bandits Chen Zhiyou and the suspected boatman Lu Huai. They were all escorted to Bengbu and handed over to the judicial section of the Changhuai Water Public Security Bureau for interrogation.
