Local News

Songhu Garrison Headquarters: Announces Martial Law in the City

Central News Agency reports that the news of the mutiny by the garrison troops in Xi'an came suddenly, and the city was shocked. However, the officials and people remained calm. Yang Hu, the Songhu Garrison Commander, in order to maintain public order and prevent petty crimes, and after receiving a telegram from the Minister of Military and Political Affairs and consulting with Mayor Wu, announced martial law in accordance with the law from today. The following is the proclamation by Commander Yang:

Songhu Garrison Headquarters Proclamation (参字第一一一三号): It is hereby ordered that the telegram from the Minister of Military and Political Affairs, He Wenxiu, reads roughly as follows: "The Xi'an garrison troops have mutinied, and I am deeply concerned that this will affect the public order in the Shanghai area. The commander should immediately declare temporary martial law," and so on. This commander, in accordance with the above, hereby declares martial law in the Shanghai area from today onwards in accordance with the martial law law. During the period of martial law, if there are any lawless elements who disrupt local order and endanger public safety, this commander will strictly punish them in accordance with the martial law law in order to curb the unrest. In addition to separately reporting this to the higher authorities, this proclamation is issued for public knowledge. This is hereby proclaimed, Commander Yang Hu, December 24th of the 25th year of the Republic of China.

Mayor Wu's Report at the City Government Yesterday: Sanctioning Rebellion to Save the Nation; Hoping Citizens Remain Calm and Support National Policy; Wishing Mr. Zhang Would Realize His Error and Consider the Overall Situation

According to the Central News Agency, the city government held its weekly memorial service yesterday morning, during which Mayor Wu reported on "Sanctioning Rebellion to Save the Nation." The original text is recorded as follows:

Comrades, today there is a very important matter to report to you. This important matter, I believe you have already seen in yesterday's and today's newspapers. This matter is the rebellion of Zhang Xueliang's troops in Xi'an on the 12th, their surrender to the Communist Party, and the encirclement of Chairman Chiang in Xi'an. This can be considered the most unfortunate and heartbreaking event in the history of China's revival. This has dealt a great blow to the construction of our new China, the revival of the Chinese nation, and the arduous work of resisting foreign aggression and saving the country. After this incident occurred, it can truly be said that "it saddens those who are close and gladdens those who are enemies."

For the past ten years, the people of China have encountered unprecedented difficulties and dangers. Fortunately, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, we have achieved what we have today amidst these unprecedented difficulties and dangers. Today's achievements, progress, and construction in China are so great and rapid that they are unmatched by any era in Chinese history. This great and rapid achievement is a ray of dawn for the revival of the Chinese nation and gives the people of the country the belief that the Chinese nation will not perish. Now, just when China's future is beginning to show a glimmer of hope, and when the domestic and foreign affairs departments have found solutions, such a heartbreaking and unfortunate event has occurred. Naturally, this has dealt a great blow to our country's future. If we do not respond properly to this blow, our country's fate will decline from this point onward. In the process of building a new China, the initial condition required is to have a leader to command it so that the strength of the whole country can be concentrated and effectively developed. The cultivation of a great leader cannot be achieved in three or four years; it requires long-term efforts. Chairman Chiang is diligent, responsible, and strives for the country. His decades of meritorious service in following the Premier, his civil and military achievements, are too numerous to mention. It is no easy feat for him to be universally loved and supported by the people. Now, let us first list the major achievements of Chairman Chiang's leadership of the people of the country in the past ten years, as follows: First, the success of the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army. Second, the establishment of the foundation of the National Government in Nanjing, providing the whole country with a unified government. Third, in the past two or three decades, the people of the country have never been able to achieve true unity, but today we have finally achieved true unity. Fourth, in the past, the people of the country passively obeyed the government. Today, the people of the country not only passively obey the government but also actively cooperate with the government and support the government. The strength of our entire country has been concentrated. Fifth, the most important aspect of China's construction is transportation. Due to China's vast territory and inconvenient transportation, all undertakings could not be implemented as scheduled. In recent years, among the active construction projects throughout the country, the most difficult one is transportation construction, such as highways and railways throughout the country, which we have already built. Sixth, the popularization of mass education, the improvement of mass knowledge, the development of national consciousness, the strict enforcement of national discipline, and the advocacy and implementation of the New Life Movement are all great works in the spiritual construction of the nation. These are some of the achievements made by Chairman Chiang in leading the people of the country during the period related to China's revival. This achievement is the foundation for the revival of the Chinese nation. Unexpectedly, today, Chairman Chiang, who is leading the people of the country to strive for national revival, is besieged by rebel troops, causing a great blow to the future of the Chinese nation's revival. This is truly a very important and heartbreaking event.

Why did Zhang Xueliang rebel? Because Zhang Xueliang is responsible for suppressing bandits in the Northwest. However, in recent years, his performance in suppressing bandits in the Northwest has not been very good. Not only is his performance in suppressing bandits poor, but his strength has also suffered considerable losses due to the suppression of bandits. Because his troops cannot suppress bandits, he feels that suppressing bandits is difficult. Because suppressing bandits is difficult, he is unwilling to suppress bandits. However, he does not say that he is unwilling to suppress bandits but uses the pretext of advocating tolerance of the Communists to cover up his failure to suppress bandits. In the process of our National Revolution, we encountered an unprecedented foreign invasion, which almost caused the people of the country to panic. At the same time, China has been plagued by the Communist Party. If we had only encountered foreign invasions in the process of the National Revolution without the disturbance of the Communist Party and the Communists' internal restraint, we believe that the current national crisis could have been resolved with considerable certainty. At the very least, we could have prevented the national crisis from escalating to its current state. The main reason why China's current national crisis is so serious, to the extent that we still do not have complete confidence in resolving the national crisis, is the Chinese Red bandits. In the past, the Chinese Red bandits disturbed the borders of provinces such as Jiangxi, Hunan, Anhui, Fujian, and Zhejiang for six or seven years, causing incalculable losses to the people of those provinces and restraining hundreds of thousands of our national troops. Since the Red bandits in Jiangxi, Hunan, Anhui, Fujian, and Zhejiang provinces were besieged by our national troops on a large scale last year, they suffered a crushing defeat and fled westward to the areas of Sichuan, Shaanxi, and Gansu, where they have been causing disturbances for two or three years, restraining many national troops. Therefore, the Communist Party has been causing disturbances in China for nearly ten years. During these ten years, not only have various parts of China suffered incalculable losses, but our national construction has also been restrained, preventing us from using all our strength to cope with foreign invasions and resolve the national crisis. Furthermore, the reason why we cannot tolerate the Communists is that, first, our most pressing need now is national self-determination and independence, while the Communists advocate class struggle and divide the strength of the nation. Second, the Communists rely on the Third International, making them red traitors and pseudo-bandits of foreign aggression. Foreign aggression is already enough to threaten China, and the Communists' internal rebellion is also a major disaster for the Chinese nation. Therefore, communism can never save China. The doctrine that truly suits China and can save China is the Three Principles of the People. If we want China not to perish, to be independent, and to revive, we must not only not tolerate the Red bandits but also fundamentally eliminate them. If we want to build a new China and revive the Chinese nation, we must eliminate the Red bandits. If we want to resist foreign aggression and save the country, we must eliminate the Red bandits. Therefore, Chairman Chiang wants to first pacify the internal situation and then resist foreign aggression, to concentrate the strength of the whole country after the domestic situation is stabilized and unite against foreign aggression. If the country is not unified and there are Red bandits causing disturbances domestically, we cannot resist foreign aggression. This is a very simple and obvious principle.

Zhang Xueliang's tolerance of the Communists this time violates our country's national policy. What is our national policy? Our national policy is to suppress bandits, eliminate traitors, resist foreign aggression, and save the country. To suppress Red bandits, eliminate traitors, resist foreign aggression, and save the country is our national policy. Zhang Xueliang's alliance with the Communists violates the national policy, which means opposing the 450 million people of the country and overturning our country against the public will of the people. His encirclement of Chairman Chiang is a major blow to the people of the country at a time when they are actively working to save themselves, seek survival, and revive the nation. This blow will not only cause our work to save ourselves and seek survival to come to a halt but also pose a great danger to the future of our country and nation. Under the current circumstances, the people of the country should realize the gravity of this matter and unite to support Chairman Chiang. They should also demand that Zhang Xueliang restore Chairman Chiang's freedom as soon as possible, so that our country does not lose its center of gravity, with a very serious attitude unanimously throughout the country. At the same time, the people of the country should also unanimously support the National Government and its national policy of suppressing bandits, eliminating traitors, resisting foreign aggression, and saving the country, and support the central government's measures to deal with Zhang Xueliang. Locally, we should strictly guard against the Communist Party and all other traitors who are causing disturbances, spreading rumors, and inciting trouble. The people of the country should understand the seriousness of the national crisis and unite under the leadership of the central government to carry out the work of suppressing bandits, eliminating traitors, resisting foreign aggression, and saving the country. They should not lightly believe rumors, disrupt their steps, and be taken advantage of by the enemy. Shanghai, in particular, is the economic center of our country, and Shanghai is of great importance to the country. The citizens of Shanghai, in addition to being deeply saddened by this unexpected blow, should be very calm and composed in dealing with this situation, await the government's handling, and the government bears full responsibility for Shanghai's security and will absolutely not allow it to have any impact on local security. I hope that the citizens of Shanghai will remain calm and composed and work together with the Shanghai Municipal Government to maintain this difficult situation. If the people of the country, especially the citizens of Shanghai, can remain calm and composed, await the government's handling of the Xi'an Incident, and unite to support the National Government and Chairman Chiang, I believe that this incident can be resolved without difficulty. Because there are many people in Zhang Xueliang's subordinates in Xi'an who are deeply aware of the righteousness, and Zhang Xueliang himself, in taking this wrong action, is probably forced by the environment and not entirely acting on his own initiative. I think he would not dare to completely disregard the public will of the people of the country and act arbitrarily. Therefore, as long as the people of the country remain calm and support the government, I dare say that this matter will be resolved quickly.

Song Ziwen Meets with Reporters and Makes Important Remarks; Whether to Go to Xi'an Awaits Government Orders; Song Remains in Shanghai at Kong's Request to Stabilize the Financial Market

Song Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council and Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, returned to Shanghai from his inspection tour of Guangdong and Guangxi the day before yesterday. At noon yesterday, he met with reporters at the Bank of China and made the following important remarks:

The Xi'an Incident Must Be Resolved Quickly

According to Song, regarding the Xi'an Incident, the news he received was the same as reported. President Chiang is absolutely safe in Xi'an. He believes that the Xi'an Incident is the most unfortunate event for the country. Currently, effective methods must be used to resolve it in the shortest possible time, as the eyes of the world are focused on China. His personal and official relationship with President Chiang and his long-standing friendship with Zhang Xueliang are well-known. In this special relationship, if there are any possible solutions, he is willing to make his best efforts under the guidance of the government. As for what methods to take, it must be decided by the government. Whether it is necessary for him to make a trip to Xi'an also awaits orders from the government. Endona has arrived in Luoyang and will soon transfer to Xi'an. He was instructed by Finance Minister Kong to stay in Shanghai to take care of financial matters. Currently, the market is relatively stable. The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications continue to buy and sell foreign exchange without restrictions.

Guangdong Province Will Develop Very Rapidly

Song continued to describe his visit to Guangdong, saying that this was his second return to Guangdong since he left with the Northern Expeditionary Army. His impressions were very deep. He recalled that during the Northern Expedition, he discussed major party and national policies in Guangdong and formulated two plans: one was to reorganize the economy of Guangdong Province to consolidate the foundation of the party and state, and the other was to launch the Northern Expedition to complete the revolution. At that time, it was decided to adopt the latter, so the Northern Expedition was launched, and the economy of Guangdong Province fell into stagnation. For several years, it was isolated from other provinces. The most obvious examples are: (1) the difference in the monetary system, and the exchange with other provinces required conversion through Hong Kong dollars, and (2) the obstruction of transportation, which was previously all by sea. Now that unification is complete and the Yuehan Railway is open to traffic, it has become one with the country economically, and its future development will be very rapid and grand.

Shanghai Financial Circles Invest in Guangdong

Discussing Guangdong's economic policy, previously, due to the state of separation, it was based on a single province. For example, Guangdong Province does not produce cotton, but it also operates its own yarn factories. Other industries also follow the principle of self-sufficiency. The people of Guangdong eat rice, but their own production is insufficient, so they rely on Siam, resulting in a huge leakage. Now that transportation has improved and unification has been completed, its economic plan naturally takes the country as a unit. This is a natural trend. Guangdong Province is rich, and its future development will be unlimited. Previously, the financial circles did not move forward because the monetary system was not unified. Now, they are investing, such as Bank of Communications, Jin City Bank, and the Mainland Bank, all of which are planning to set up branches. Recently, because food rice has been manipulated by merchants, and grain prices have risen, the provincial authorities are negotiating with the financial circles to transport Hunan rice to regulate the people's food supply. From this alone, it can be seen that the revival of Guangdong Province and the general economic and financial relations of the country are interrelated.

Development Plans Emphasize Various Points

Zhu also said that he had visited Hainan Island, and there were two reasons for this: he was originally from Wenchang County, Hainan, and conveniently returned to his hometown to visit, and the island's special position in China's economy made it necessary to seek development. Song said that he had spoken in detail to reporters in Wenchang, which he believed had been reported. However, in general, although our country is vast and rich in resources, only Hainan Island has tropical products, such as rubber trees, betel nuts, coffee, and rich minerals, especially tin. Our country has a huge trade deficit every year, and many tropical products are imported. Developing the island can recover a lot of leakage, and its importance to the domestic economy can be imagined. As for the most important development plans, they are: 1. Opening up seaports and building ports near Haikou. 2. Building a railway from the seaport east through Wenchang to the south of the island to facilitate the transportation of products, costing approximately 25 million to 30 million yuan. In Guangdong Province, it is planned to build the Yuegui Railway to reach Fujian in the east and Jiangxi in the north, which is very important economically and defensively, costing approximately 44.5 million yuan. The Huangpu Port is planned to be built into a second-class port. The first step is to deepen the Pearl River so that merchant ships of 8,000 to 9,000 tons can enter and exit the port, at a cost of approximately 6 million yuan. Subsequent progress will involve the construction of wharves, warehouses, and railways. The provincial authorities are actively carrying out the above plans, and the National Economic Council will provide technical assistance in the future.

Guangxi's Way Out Lies in Minerals

Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi are both old friends. He was invited to Guangxi for a pleasant gathering and conveniently inspected Guangxi's economic situation. He did not discuss any political or financial issues. Guangxi is extremely poor, but the province is well-organized, so it can cope with economic difficulties. Guangxi was originally a province with a trade deficit, but recently, it has worked hard to produce and resist the import of luxury goods, which has reduced the amount of the trade deficit. Guangxi has many minerals, and its economic way out in the future should be in this area. After the reform of the monetary system in Guangxi, the financial circles will rush to set up branches, just like the current situation in Guangdong Province.

After the Xi'an Incident, Shanghai-Shaanxi Remittances Continue as Usual; Eurasia Aircraft Cease Landing in Xi'an; Longhai Railway Stops Operations; Telegraphs Above Tongguan Still Not Open Last Night

After the Xi'an Incident, remittances between Shanghai and Shaanxi were still accepted by various banks. Shanghai-Xinjiang aircraft stopped landing in Xi'an and other places. Telegraph communications between Shanghai and Shaanxi were still not open above Tongguan as of last night. The details are as follows:

Shanghai-Shaanxi Remittances Continue to Be Accepted

Xi'an is the capital of Shaanxi Province. The Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, China Farmers' Bank, and Shanghai Bank all have branches there to handle domestic remittances. Since the Xi'an Incident, regarding remittances from Shanghai to various places in Shaanxi Province, a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency inquired with the Bank of China last night. All of the above banks are still accepting remittances as usual. However, since the industry believes that Xi'an and other places are very chaotic, remittances are temporarily being observed, and the amount has therefore decreased sharply.

Land and Air Transportation Are Affected

Although the Eurasia Airlines' Shanghai-Xinjiang aircraft are still flying as usual, they have stopped landing in Xi'an when passing through. As for the Lanzhou-Baotou line, the Ningxia-Lanzhou section has been suspended. The company has not received reports on the Baotou-Ningxia section. After the Longhai Railway temporarily opened to Huayin, freight cars on the railway were temporarily suspended due to busy transportation. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has reduced the number of ships traveling to Lianyungang.

Telegraphs Above Tongguan Are Blocked

According to news from the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications yesterday, telegraphs in Shaanxi Province above Tongguan, such as Xi'an, Lanzhou, Huayin, Chishui, Weinan, Lingkou, Xinfeng, Lintong, Xianyang, Baishui, , Jiji, Pucheng, and Sanyuan, were still blocked and not open as of last night. However, telegraphs in various places along the Longhai Railway below Tongguan were open as usual.

Emergency Meeting of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions; Strictly Preventing Labor Disputes

Order to Not Neglect Work or Strike; Order to Strictly Prevent Reactionary Elements

Yesterday, the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions held an emergency meeting of the Executive Committee for the Xi'an Incident to discuss countermeasures, decided to strictly prevent the occurrence of labor disputes, and prevent the activities of reactionary elements. The details are as follows:

Measures Decided at the Emergency Meeting

The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions convened an emergency meeting of the Executive Committee at 10:00 AM yesterday, attended by Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Na Xubai, Ye Xianggao, Zhang Kechang, Long Peiyun, Gong Yuting, Li Hua, and more than a dozen others. First, Chairman Zhu Xuefan reported on the sudden outbreak of the Xi'an Incident, which caused nationwide outrage. The Federation had already telegraphed Zhang Xueliang to rein in his horse on the brink of the precipice. In order to prevent the activities of reactionary elements, this meeting was convened again to discuss measures. The following cases were resolved: (1) To convene a meeting of various trade unions on the 15th to report on the incident and hope that the comrades in the labor community will deal with it calmly. (2) To order various trade unions to strictly prevent reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to be active and absolutely avoid the occurrence of labor disputes. (3) To petition the party and government agencies to jointly issue a notice, severely warning capital in this critical period not to lay off workers or reduce wages, causing disputes. (4) To telegraph national mass organizations, requesting them to send representatives to Xi'an to personally persuade Zhang Xueliang to cease hostilities and restore Chairman Chiang's freedom. (5) To unite with groups such as the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and local associations to concentrate steps and jointly deal with the emergency incident, and to push Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, and Shao Xubai to contact separately.

Order Various Trade Unions to Strictly Prevent Labor Disputes

The Municipal Federation of Trade Unions issued an order to all affiliated trade unions in the city yesterday, stating, "In order to issue a notice, the Xi'an Incident has occurred, and the situation is extremely critical. Our city's workers should take a calm and composed attitude, quietly await the proper handling by the central government, and strictly prevent reactionary elements from taking the opportunity to be active to maintain local order. If there are any labor-capital disputes in various industries, they should be submitted to the party and government agencies for mediation in accordance with legal procedures. It is absolutely forbidden to neglect work or strike, causing labor disputes, and giving villains an opportunity to take advantage of. In addition to submitting it to the Municipal Party Department and the Municipal Government, please issue a joint notice, severely warning the capital of various industries not to take the opportunity to lay off workers or reduce wages, causing disputes. It is ordered that various trade unions immediately order the affiliated workers to comply with it together. This order."

Five Organizations Including the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and Local Associations

We believe that Chairman Chiang is the commander-in-chief of the entire country and his safety is of utmost importance. Zhu Qinglan

To Zhang Hanqing, my younger brother from Xi'an, and all military division commanders, brigade commanders, and regimental commanders of the Northeast Army, I have just heard that your troops suddenly disagreed with Chiang Kai-shek and detained him in Xi'an. Hanxue Society

Yesterday, the Shanghai Hanxue Society telegraphed Zhang Xueliang, saying, "To Mr. Zhang Hanqing of Xi'an, As the Suiyuan Incident unfolds and the nation faces dire difficulties, we are shocked to hear that you have seized the commander-in-chief and staged a military coup. Since the establishment of the Republic of China in 1911, the country and its people have suffered from internal strife for nearly twenty years. Fortunately, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, with the people's interests at heart and peace as his guiding principle, has strived for unification and construction, leading to the situation we have today. Efforts such as economic recovery, preparations for resisting aggression, and large-scale construction are all entrusted by the people of the whole country to Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, with the expectation of rapid completion, which you are well aware of. We never expected that you would suddenly disrupt this progress with such an unfortunate incident. We are truly perplexed and cannot understand. If the above-mentioned great plans for national revival and resisting aggression are not correct, why do you not express your great views so that public opinion can choose whether they are correct or not? If the progress of the above-mentioned national salvation endeavors is not fast enough, you have served the party and the country for many years, so why have we not seen you propose any plans beforehand? As for the chances of success in international relations, one should decide after the start of a national war based on the opportune moment. If it is the will of all the people, it cannot be violated by one or two military leaders. If it is what all the people hate, it cannot be monopolized by one or two military leaders. Therefore, your action of detaining the commander-in-chief has nothing to do with the goals you seek. We do not know why you must take this path. Furthermore, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek's leadership position today depends on the collective strength of the people of the whole country. The convergence of the power of the people of the whole country also depends on Mr. Chiang Kai-shek's long-term, continuous, and practical efforts for the welfare of the country and the people. His immense power is built on the collective strength and trust of the people. To seize what the people trust will surely be hated by the people. Since ancient times, none who have done this have escaped destruction. If you are truly for the country and the people, why do you not present your decisions, using peaceful means that do not endanger the foundation of the nation, and submit them to public opinion to determine their acceptance or rejection? At the same time, you should immediately restore the freedom of the supreme commander, so as not to cause significant losses to the future of national defense in the process. In this way, your sincerity and enthusiasm can be fully demonstrated to the masses, and you can gain the understanding of the people of the country. Moreover, we have seen Mr. Chiang Kai-shek's consistent pursuit of peace in the handling of the situation in the Southwest this autumn. We believe you have also already considered this and have no concerns. In this era, if military force can be used for personal gain, then Mr. Chiang Kai-shek would no longer be detained by you. How can you guarantee that no one will follow your example in the future? Time is fleeting and does not allow for delay. This special telegram is sent in the hope that you will accept it. Respectfully, the Shanghai Hanxue Society."

Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng has not been feeling well recently. The doctor has advised him to rest for a few days. He has declined all social engagements. All important documents are still being processed as usual.

Expanded Commemorative Week at the Municipal Party Headquarters Yesterday: The People Should Recognize the Effort, Tao Baichuan's Report Excerpts: Enumerating Zhang Xueliang's Wrongs

According to the National Society, the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters convened more than 500 representatives from various district branches yesterday morning to hold an expanded commemorative week. Standing Committee member Tao Baichuan gave an important report on the current situation. Excerpts from his speech are as follows: (1) On the 12th of this month, Zhang Xueliang suddenly rebelled in Xi'an, leading his troops, while simultaneously detaining Chairman Chiang and issuing a circular telegram advocating the overthrow of the National Government. The Central Government has appropriate measures to deal with this, and all provinces are loyal to the Central Government. Chairman Chiang is currently safe, which is a blessing in disguise. (2) Upon investigation, there are few reasons for Zhang Xueliang's rebellion. Although it is said to be for political reasons, Zhang Xueliang is actually an incompetent Liu A Dou. What politics does he understand? His rebellion is primarily because the Central Government wanted him to suppress the Red bandits, and in order to preserve his power, he not only did not want to suppress the Red bandits, but colluded with them. At the same time, to cover up his mistakes, he chanted the slogan of not suppressing the Red bandits. Therefore, this incident is entirely an old trick of old-style warlords resisting the Central Government to maintain their territories. (3) Zhang Xueliang's circular telegram said that he wanted to fight back to his old home in the Northeast. This is clearly a deception. Who would believe that someone who did not defend his old home in the Northeast and handed it over to others could fight back to the Northeast? Moreover, to fight back to his old home, one must support the leader, consolidate the Central Government, unite internally, and strengthen national power before there is any way to do so. His actions are to overthrow the leader, overthrow the Central Government, dissolve internal unity, and eliminate national power. At worst, China may become a second Spain. How can he fight back to his old home? The Northeast was destroyed by Zhang Xueliang himself. He destroyed the Northeast in the past, and now he is destroying the Northwest. He is truly a sinner of the nation. Can we, the people, tolerate the actions of this sinner? (4) Zhang Xueliang's circular telegram said that he wanted to unite with the Communist Party. This is an extremely dangerous proposal. The Communist Party's background is in the Third International, and the Communist Party's position is class struggle. What China needs now is to make a national self-determination and national independence movement. We cannot allow class struggle to eliminate the power of national struggle. We cannot let the Third International decide our national destiny. Therefore, we cannot unite with the Communist Party. We cannot unite with the traitors of white imperialism, and we cannot unite with the tools of the Second International. (5) Zhang Xueliang's circular telegram said that he wanted to ally with Russia. We should first consider whether Russia has the necessity and determination to wage war against Japan, whether Russia is willing to unite with China, and whether Russia has the power to help China. We have reason to believe that (a) because Japan is trying its best to befriend Russia, because Russia has no reason to fight Japan, and because Russia in Europe is heavily constrained by Italy and Germany, the Soviet Union currently has no determination to wage war against Japan. We admit that expressing friendship and goodwill to the Soviet Union is something that the current government has been diligently doing for a long time, without waiting for Zhang Xueliang to propose it, let alone detaining the leader and rebelling. (6) In short, Zhang Xueliang's rebellion is ungrateful to Chairman Chiang, rebellious against the Central Government, colluding with the Red bandits and the Communist Party, continuing to endanger China, and helping the bandits and puppets in Chahar and Suiyuan to boost their arrogance, destroying our Great Wall. He is suffering from unrequited love for the Soviet Union, and he is digging his own grave. The losses suffered by China as a result are truly unimaginable. Zhang Xueliang is truly a sinner of the country and the nation. (7) Our current tasks are: (a) to reaffirm our support for Chairman Chiang and demand that Zhang Xueliang immediately and unconditionally restore all of Chairman Chiang's freedom; (b) to reaffirm our support for the National Government and its national policy of suppressing bandits, eliminating traitors, resisting foreign aggression, and saving the country; (c) to support the Central Government's measures to punish Zhang Xueliang; (d) to strictly prevent the Red bandits and the Communist Party, as well as all other traitors, from disturbing the local area; (e) not to allow the Red bandits and the Communist Party, as well as all other traitors, to mix with the people, spread rumors, and incite them; (f) the people should understand the severity of the national crisis and must, under the leadership of the Central Government, carry out the work of suppressing bandits, eliminating traitors, resisting foreign aggression, and saving the country, and must not easily believe rumors, disrupt their own steps, and be taken advantage of by the enemy. (8) The party and the country are at this serious beginning. All comrades of our party should devote themselves to the party and the country. First, lead the people to do the above six points. Second, everyone must take on the responsibility of the police and detectives to prevent all enemies from shaking people's hearts and undermining security. As the saying goes, "A scholar's integrity is seen in poverty, and a hero is known in times of chaos." Now is the time for us to be tested. May our comrades work hard.

After the Xi'an Incident, Securities Market Suspended Trading Yesterday

Brokers' Request to Stop Trading Unsuccessful

Cotton Yarn, Flour, and Gold Prices Soared

Central, China, and Communications Banks Meeting to Maintain Foreign Exchange

Since the Xi'an Incident occurred, the Securities Brokers Association held a general meeting yesterday, requesting that trading be suspended, but was unsuccessful. After the opening, all stocks fell, resulting in a suspension of trading. The prices of cotton yarn, flour, miscellaneous grains, and gold all soared. The Central, China, and Communications Banks held a meeting to make every effort to maintain foreign exchange. Details are as follows:

Securities Brokers Hold General Meeting

Twenty-two members of the Chinese Securities Exchange Brokers Association, including Dakangcheng, believing that the abduction of Chairman Chiang in Xi'an had a great impact on the financial market, sent a letter to the association requesting an extraordinary emergency meeting. The association approved this and held a general meeting of members at 9:00 AM yesterday in the association's 8th-floor auditorium. Fifty-six brokers attended, chaired by Chairman Zhu Anfu. The brokers said that the situation was extraordinary and advocated a temporary suspension of trading, requesting the Exchange's Board of Directors to submit a request to the Ministry of Finance and the Supervisor for approval. A letter was immediately sent to the Board of Directors for processing. Later, the Board of Directors replied that since the exchanges of various industries were operating as usual, the industry was inconvenient to be unique. After the brokers' meeting ended, the stock exchange had already rung the bell to open. The meeting was declared adjourned.

All Stocks Suspended After Opening

The Securities Exchange rang the bell to open at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. The market was very chaotic, and people were uneasy. After the opening, all types of unified government bonds (A, B, C, D, and E) fell by four yuan and were suspended. Type E bonds for December and January were 58.5 yuan, Type D bonds for December and January were 59.5 yuan, Type C bonds for December and January were 58.5 yuan, Type B bonds for December and January were 161.5 yuan, and Type A bonds for December and January were 69 yuan. However, the 96 government bonds opened as usual in the morning and afternoon. The final closing price for the December issue was 7.3 yuan, down 1.5 yuan from the previous day. The January issue closed at 7.6 yuan, down 1.15 yuan from the previous day.

Cotton Yarn Trading Soared

The Chinese Cotton Yarn Exchange opened as usual at 9:30 AM yesterday morning. The market was very chaotic. Standing Director Wen Lanting personally supervised the market. (1) The opening price for December yarn was 248 yuan, down 5.1 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for January was 239 yuan, down 1.9 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for February was 240 yuan, up 5.5 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for March was 240 yuan, up 6.5 yuan from the previous day. (2) The opening price for December cotton was 44 yuan, up 1.445 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for January was 44.5 yuan, up 1.4 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for February was 45 yuan, up 1.4 yuan from the previous day. The opening price for March was 45.2 yuan, up 1.25 yuan from the previous day. In the last afternoon session, (1) the closing price for yarn was 258 yuan for December, 245 yuan for January, 239.3 yuan for February, and 239 yuan for March. (2) The closing price for cotton was 43.4 yuan for December, 44 yuan for January, 44.55 yuan for February, and 44.8 yuan for March.

Gold Trading Prices Rose Slightly

The Shanghai Gold Exchange opened as usual at 9:00 AM yesterday morning. The opening price was 1,158 yuan, and it immediately rose, once passing the 1,170 yuan mark, before falling back. The closing price at 11:40 AM was 1,164.2 yuan. Since the government cracked down on speculation, trading at the Gold Exchange has sharply decreased.

Three Banks Made Efforts to Promote Foreign Exchange

The Central, China, and Communications Banks made every effort to maintain foreign exchange and did not allow other problems to arise due to the Xi'an Incident. After the meeting held on the day before yesterday afternoon and the meeting yesterday morning by Xi Demao of the Central Bank, Bei Songsun of the China Bank, and Zhang Peishen of the Communications Bank, it was decided that the three banks would continue to buy and sell foreign exchange without restriction, based on the past policy of stabilizing foreign exchange, due to adequate preparation. The foreign exchange rates announced by the Central Bank this morning were: 1 shilling and 2.5 pence for London, 30 US dollars for New York, 630 francs for Paris, 73.5 marks for Berlin, 103 yen for Japan, and 97 Hong Kong dollars for Hong Kong. Trading was very active.

Prices of Miscellaneous Grains Rose

Yesterday, the market prices at the Miscellaneous Grains and Oil Cake Exchange were higher than on Saturday. Wheat for December rose by 0.17 yuan, January rose by 0.2 yuan, February rose by 0.24 yuan, March rose by 0.23 yuan, and April rose by 0.22 yuan. Sesame in the morning rose by 0.5 yuan for December and 0.55 yuan for January. Trading was suspended in the afternoon. Soybean oil rose by 1.05 yuan for December, 0.85 yuan for January, 1.1 yuan for February, 1.1 yuan for March, and 1.15 yuan for April. Soybean cake rose by 0.0675 yuan for February, 0.075 yuan for March, 0.0725 yuan for April, and 0.0725 yuan for May.

Regulations on Limit Up/Down

The Miscellaneous Grain Exchange also issued Public Notice No. 107 on bean cakes yesterday, stipulating measures for suspending trading due to limit up/down. The original text reads: "Due to the current situation, in order to stabilize the market prices in the exchange, the daily rise and fall of each unit shall not exceed 1 yuan for soybean oil, 0.2 yuan for beans, wheat, and sesame, and 0.1 yuan for soybean cake. If the limit is exceeded, part or all of the trading will be suspended and will not be recorded in the accounts. This is hereby announced."

Closing Price of Flour Also Rose

Yesterday, the market prices for flour rose. The closing price in the morning rose by 0.095 yuan for December, and rose another 0.05 yuan in the afternoon. January rose by 0.0825 yuan in the morning and rose another 0.0375 yuan in the afternoon. February rose by 0.1075 yuan in the morning and rose another 0.055 yuan in the afternoon. March rose by 0.1425 yuan in the morning and rose another 0.01 yuan in the afternoon. April rose by 0.145 yuan in the morning. The closing prices for the last session yesterday are recorded as follows: 4.288 yuan for December, 4.2875 yuan for January, 4.301 yuan for February, 4.303 yuan for March, and 4.303 yuan for April.

He completed his duties and left Nanjing on the 11:00 PM night express train the night before last, returning to Shanghai yesterday morning at about 7:00 AM, alighting at the North Station and returning to the consulate on Avenue Joffre to rest and resume work as usual.

After the first two batches of 8,006 crates of antiquities stored at the Palace Museum in Shanghai were transported to Nanjing, the third batch was transported again yesterday morning at 6:00 AM. The Maotai Foreign Firm was once again entrusted to handle the transportation, hiring fifteen trucks to transport the crates in batches to the Meigen Road Station and load them onto the designated special train. However, because the number of special train carriages was too small, loading was completed at 4:00 PM, with a total of more than 2,200 crates loaded. The special train departed at 8:00 PM to transport the antiquities to the preservation institute in Nanjing. The French Concession Police and the Municipal Public Security Bureau dispatched police officers and detectives to strengthen security on Tianzhutang Street and at the Meigen Road Station.

Muslims Complete Fasting Period, Eid al-Fitr Today

Muslims in Shanghai fast (abstain from food) for one month every year in September according to the Chinese calendar. They begin fasting before dawn and stop eating during the day, only breaking the fast after sunset. Today (the 15th) marks the end of the Muslims' fasting period. This morning, Muslims will gather at various mosques to hold a grand ceremony. Before the ceremony, Muslims must first perform ablutions, wear new clothes, and give alms (to help the poor) before going to the mosque for the ceremony and praying for world peace.

Cai Yuanpei's Illness Improving

The condition of Cai Yuanpei, President of the Academia Sinica, has improved again yesterday. His temperature, pulse, and blood pressure have gradually returned to normal. However, he still needs to pay close attention to his recuperation. All visiting guests are declined from meeting the patient in accordance with the doctor's instructions.

Local Association Holds Winter Conference Today

The Local Association of Shanghai is deeply concerned about the Xi'an Incident. It held an emergency meeting the other day and agreed that the directors and members could come to the association every day from 3:00 PM to 4:00 PM within the next few days to inquire or exchange opinions. Yesterday afternoon at about 3:00 PM, the directors and members arrived one after another, including Du Yuesheng, Wang Xiaolai, Qian Xinzhi, Mu Piaochu, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Pan Yangyao, and Zou Bingwen, among others. An informal discussion was held to exchange information and a copy of the telegram sent by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce and the five public groups to Xi'an was circulated among them. It was also decided that the association would send another telegram to Deputy Chairman Yan of Taiyuan to jointly find ways to rescue Chairman Chiang and to continue to strive for the military campaign to suppress bandits in Suiyuan. The association also scheduled a winter conference at 5:00 PM this afternoon to report on association affairs and to discuss the current situation in detail.

Finnish President's Birthday, Finnish Consul General Hosts Guests

Shanghai Finns Hold Public Banquet

Today is the 75th birthday of Mr. Svinhufvud, the first President of the Republic of Finland. Mr. Nicklin, the Acting Consul General of Finland in Shanghai, will hold a celebration at 301 Maersin Road this morning. Chinese and foreign officials and celebrities in Shanghai will all go to congratulate him. At 8:00 PM in the evening, the Finnish community in Shanghai will hold a congratulatory public banquet. President Svinhufvud has made great contributions to Finland. In his youth, he served as a lawyer and a local judge. Since engaging in the revolution in 1917, he has gained the faith of the people and was subsequently elected as the Prime Minister of the new government. He retired from 1918 to 1930, and was elected as President in May 1931.

Shanghai Municipal Anti-Tuberculosis Exhibition

Opening Today at the Wuzhou Pharmacy

The China Anti-Tuberculosis Association, recognizing the severe harm and rapid spread of tuberculosis, is not only advocating preventive measures and informing all sectors of society to promote prevention, but also recognizing that the general public often overlooks the subtle onset of tuberculosis, delaying initial diagnosis and ultimately succumbing to the bacteria, which is deeply regrettable. Therefore, it has partnered with Wuzhou Pharmacy to host an anti-tuberculosis exhibition, using rich materials and eye-catching displays to ensure that all attendees understand preventive measures. It is reported that the exhibition content is exceptionally rich, including statistical tables of tuberculosis mortality rates in various countries, comparative tables of tuberculosis mortality rates in various parts of China, hygiene posters, various tuberculosis specimens, human models, lung models, comparisons of tuberculous and healthy lungs, intestinal tuberculosis models, tubercle bacilli under a microscope, artificial pneumothorax and X-ray photographs, various forms of old tuberculosis, glass slides, ward designs, nutritious foods, anti-tuberculosis books, and everything else. All those concerned about anti-tuberculosis work and health should pay attention to it. Furthermore, Wuzhou Pharmacy, to increase audience interest, will also distribute complimentary tickets and gifts to attendees as souvenirs. It is also reported that the association will hold an opening ceremony at 2:00 PM today on the sixth floor of Wuzhou Pharmacy. The order is as follows: (1) Opening ceremony, (2) Opening remarks by Chairman Lu Bohong, (3) Address by the Mayor, (4) Addresses by representatives of Party and government organs, Director Pan Gongzhan, Director Li Ting'an, (5) Singing of the anti-tuberculosis song, Daotong Girls' Middle School, (6) Report by Mr. Tong Xingmen, (7) Singing of the "Don't Spit" song, Qinghua Middle School, (8) Refreshments, (9) Photography, (10) Adjournment.

Furthermore, the joint meeting of directors and supervisors of the China Anti-Tuberculosis Association is scheduled to be held at 12:00 PM today on the sixth floor of Wuzhou Pharmacy. Directors Wu Tiecheng, Lu Bohong, Li Ting'an, Pan Gongzhan, Kai Fuqing, Weng Zhilong, Huang Zifang, Chen Heqin, Wang Xiaoying, GH'Jordon, Shi Siming, etc., and supervisors Du Yuesheng, Yu Qiaqing, Pang Jingzhou, Ding Fubao, Qian Xinzhi, Yao Mulian, and Liu Zhan'en, etc., will all attend to discuss important proposals such as improving the dining movement, implementing anti-tuberculosis masks, and the national barber industry hygiene regulations.

Red Cross Society Appeals for Donations of First Aid Medicine Kits

Since the China Red Cross Society unified the organization of the Suiyuan war relief efforts nationwide, many doctors from various places have actively participated. Therefore, there are many talented people at the front line. However, due to the shortage of materials in North China, they all rely on supplies from Shanghai. Each member of the rescue team in Suiyuan must have a medicine kit containing three categories of supplies: (1) surgical instruments, (2) dressing supplies, (3) medicines, all of which are indispensable for rescue work. The quantities have been determined and calculated, and the original cost is 10 yuan in national currency per kit. Now that the society's existing reserves have been successively transported to the front, they are still insufficient for distribution. If a major war occurs, they will be even more needed. We hope that our countrymen and gentlemen will generously donate medicine kits or money to purchase them. With a small amount of money, countless lives can be saved, humanity can be protected, and the nation can be relieved. We urge everyone to quickly initiate donations. Please contact the Red Cross Society on Xinzha Road, or call 34366 for a detailed response.

Meeting Minutes of the National Accountants Association

The National Accountants Association held its fourth board meeting yesterday at its office at No. 59 Hong Kong Road. Board members Xi Yushu, Jiang Wanping, Xie Lin, Chen Riping, He Yuanming, Wang Haifan, Wang Sifang, Bei Zuyi, Lang Junwei, Wen Yiyou (Jiang representing), Chen Chaolun (Xi representing) attended. Chairman Xie Lin presided over the meeting. (A) Reporting Matters: 5 items (omitted). (B) Discussion Matters: (1) "Upon investigation, the number, names, and brief resumes of the assistant accountants when accountants apply for registration are clearly stipulated in the Accountants Regulations as matters that should be registered. However, the transfer of this registration to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce by local industrial and commercial administrative offices varies in speed. Registered accountants and their assistants have no registration certificates to prove their registration. Furthermore, assistants with diplomas in commercial or economic fields from specialized schools need to prove their years of service with the registration date. It is proposed to request the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to instruct industrial and commercial administrative offices nationwide to issue a registration certificate to accountants and their assistants upon registration, listing their names, brief resumes, and registration date separately to serve as proof. In addition, it is requested to add the above method to the implementation rules of the Accountants Regulations for permanent compliance." (Resolved) Passed. Director Xie Lin was appointed to draft the petition. (2) "Upon investigation, the organization procedures, establishment date, and list of past officers and membership numbers of each member association are not on file in this association for reference. Should the association draft a form and send it to each association for completion?" (Resolved) Director Bei Zuyi was appointed to draft the form. (3) "Various income tax regulations are currently planned to be compiled into a booklet and distributed to each member association for forwarding to members for reference." (Resolved) 1,000 copies will be printed and distributed to each association immediately.

Sworn Brothers Accuse Each Other

Xu Xuehui, a native of Songjiang and former director of the Gansu Opium Prohibition Bureau, had his face splashed with nitric acid in March of this year on Wangzhi Road in the French Concession. Gao Jinsheng, the perpetrator, was arrested on the spot and sentenced to four years of imprisonment by the Second Special Court, and is currently appealing. However, Xu suddenly filed a complaint with the Shanghai District Court, accusing Zhu Guanghan, a wealthy businessman from the same hometown, of instigating Chen Axi to instruct Gao Jinsheng to cause harm, requesting punishment, and demanding compensation of 10,000 yuan for damages. Zhu Guanghan also filed a ten-point defense, stating that he and the plaintiff were sworn brothers for more than ten years, and that recently, due to unsuccessful loan applications, the plaintiff had fabricated accusations and attempted extortion. He also hired attorney Gu Changyuan to file a counterclaim for false accusation. After the court received the complaint, Judge Wu Deying presided over the trial. However, Judge Wu was transferred to the Xuzhou Jiangsu Higher Branch Court by order of the Ministry, so Judge Yu Deren has taken over the trial. Recently, Judge Yu was also transferred to be an execution judge, so the case is now being handled by Judge Liu Bojun, who has scheduled a retrial for the 16th of this month.

Page 12

Gu Zhuxuan May Be Released Soon; Second Special Court Has Approved 20,000 Yuan Bail; Gao Third Branch Court Ruling Will Be Issued Soon

Gu Zhuxuan, a native of Yancheng, was arrested on the Mid-Autumn Festival of 1934 on suspicion of instigating the assassination of Tang Jiapeng. After a preliminary trial by the Second Special Court, he was sentenced to 15 years in prison and deprived of his civil rights for ten years. Upon appeal to the Gao Third Branch Court, the original verdict was overturned, and he was declared innocent. However, during the final stage of the appeal trial at the Gao Third Branch Court, another prisoner accused Gu of bribing the guards and bribing Zhao Guangfu and Zhang Tinggui, known as Xiao Sizi, to recant their confession of instigating perjury. He was also accused of smoking opium in the prison hospital outside Guangci Hospital. The prosecutor of the Second Special Court and the Police Department separately filed public lawsuits. His instigation to perjury case is currently under trial. The opium case has concluded after two trials by the Second Special Court and the Gao Third Branch Court, and he was sentenced to eight months in prison and deprived of his civil rights for one year. The opium case has been sent to prison for execution, with the sentence expiring on January 12 of next year. Gu had previously requested that the time he spent in detention last year be deducted from his sentence, but this was rejected by the Gao Third Branch Court. Gu then applied to the prosecutor of the Gao Third Branch Court for a reduction in his sentence, which was approved by the prosecutor. He then requested a reduction in his sentence from the Criminal Division, which was approved by the Criminal Division, granting a one-month reduction in his sentence. Therefore, Gu has now been released from prison and transferred to the detention center. However, because the Police Department was dissatisfied with Gu's acquittal in the murder case, they requested the prosecutor of the Gao Third Branch Court to appeal to the Supreme Court. The instigation to perjury case is being retried by Judge Chen Shuoying of the Second Special Court, and the trial has not yet concluded. Gu has now submitted a statement to the Gao Third Branch Court and the Second Special Court, which has been approved, allowing him to find two reputable guarantors and provide a 20,000 yuan guarantee to stop the detention. The ruling from the Gao Third Branch Court has not yet been issued, but it is expected to be approved. Gu's family is rushing to complete the bail procedures. Within ten days, Gu may regain his freedom.

Cai Fu-fu Accused of Obstructing Family

Court to Resume Hearing Shortly

I, Cai Fu-fu, also known as Cai Xuzhou, have operated the Ming Yue Lou teahouse on Xiaolin Road, Mabai Road in western Shanghai for many years. Although Cai is over forty years old, he still has a fondness for women. On April 11th of this year, he lured Jin Di, the daughter of Wang Yegen, who resides at No. [Number] in the vegetable market alley on Shenglu Road, to the Hongxiang Hotel for illicit relations. This was discovered by the girl's father, who, together with his wife, rushed to the hotel and apprehended the two. At that time, Cai immediately sought mediation to settle the matter. However, on May 11th, Jin Di suddenly disappeared again. After investigation by Wang Yegen, it was learned that Cai had lured her away again, but her whereabouts remained unknown, making it impossible to report her disappearance to the authorities. It was not until November 16th that Jin Di was found to have died suddenly at the home of her uncle, Chen Xinglin. It is rumored that this resulted from Cai's drunken misconduct. Therefore, Wang immediately reported the matter to the Caojiadu Public Security Bureau, which detained Cai. Jin Di's body was sent to the court for examination. Although the result indicated death from illness, Wang believes that Cai and Chen conspired to seduce his daughter and has filed a separate complaint with the local court, accusing Cai of obstructing family. The court accepted the complaint and issued two summonses. However, because key witnesses Yin Jubaobao and Cai Futang's wife have not yet come forward, the hearing was postponed. It is reported that the case will be resumed shortly.

Child Accidentally Eats Opium, Dies from Poisoning

Liang Jinchun, a 60-year-old Cantonese man, currently works at the Nanjing Capital Grand Theater. Five years ago in Shanghai, he took a Suzhou woman, Shi (22 years old this year), as his concubine. Over the past five years, they have had three sons. The eldest son is five years old this year, the second son is four years old, and the youngest son, A Xin, is just two years old. Liang is in Nanjing, while Shi lives with the three children in a three-story building at No. B442, Xinmin Village, Malang Road in the French Concession. A few days ago, Shi suddenly suffered from a headache and purchased a small box of opium, costing [Number] jiao, to make headache paste. The remaining opium paste was placed on a table. On the night of the [Number]th, Shi's youngest son, A Xin, played with the paste and asked for a biscuit. Shi did not notice that the biscuit in the child's hand was contaminated with the paste. As a result, he was poisoned. At seven o'clock the next morning, the child had a seizure due to the poisoning. Shi then realized what had happened and immediately sent him to Guangci Hospital. However, the child's internal organs had been severely damaged by the poison, and treatment was ineffective. He died at two o'clock yesterday morning. The hospital reported the incident to the French police, who dispatched detectives to investigate. The child's body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall for examination. Wang Ren, the prosecutor of the Special Second Court, and a court police officer went to the hall and confirmed that the death of Liang A Xin was indeed due to accidental opium poisoning. The body was handed over to the mother for burial.

Yang Zhongfen Case: Litigation Unresolved; Liu Huizhen Sues for Son's Upbringing Expenses, Claiming $9,600

Yang Zhongfen, a secretary at the Zhongnan Bank from Fujian, previously cohabitated with Liu Huizhen, a prostitute from the Meiyu brothel. Subsequently, a son was born, named A Li. However, after A Li's birth, Yang suddenly abandoned both Liu and A Li. Liu filed an abandonment lawsuit against Yang in the First Special District Court. After a trial, the court sentenced Yang to six months imprisonment, with a suspended sentence. Yang was dissatisfied with the verdict and appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court, but the appeal was rejected. Now, Liu has filed a lawsuit in the Civil Division of the First Special District Court, claiming that A Li is one year old and that the costs from now until his adulthood will be substantial. She argues that Yang should bear these costs, and therefore requests the court to order Yang to pay A Li's upbringing expenses of 50 yuan per month until he reaches the age of sixteen, totaling 9,600 yuan in national currency. This case was originally handled by Judge Tao Dejun, but due to Judge Tao's illness, Judge Xu Fuji is acting as a proxy. Yesterday, the Fourth Civil Division held a hearing, issuing an order for a further hearing at a later date.

Robbery Case on Shanhai Pass Road: One Thief Apprehended

Victim's Losses Valued at One Thousand Gold

At around 7 p.m. last night, four bandits suddenly went to the residence of a [Surname] family at No. 817, Shanhai Pass Road, to carry out a robbery. Only two of the bandits carried handguns. After entering the house, they confined all the men and women inside, and then began to search and loot. They left after about half an hour, having stolen property worth more than four thousand gold. However, when the bandits left the house, the police on duty in the area had already received a report. Upon seeing the bandits escaping, they ordered them to stop. In desperation, the bandits fired a shot. The police returned fire, knocking down one of the bandits and seizing a handgun. The remaining bandits escaped. The apprehended bandit was immediately taken to the police station, pending the capture of his accomplices.

House Collapse on Zhejiang Road Injures People

A house belonging to the Yiyuan pawnshop at the intersection of Zhejiang Road and Xiamen Road in the Public Concession was in disrepair. Workers were hired to repair it a few days ago. Unexpectedly, at around 10 p.m. last night, the high wall along the road suddenly collapsed with a crash. Some pedestrians were buried in the rubble. Patrol officers who heard the noise arrived and reported the incident to the Lao Zha Police Station, which dispatched detectives to the scene to maintain order. The injured pedestrians were sent to Renji Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, their injuries were not serious, and they were discharged after being bandaged. The collapse of the wall blocked traffic, which was quickly restored.

Municipal Health Bureau Organizes Maternal and Infant Health Services

Li Yan'an, Director of the Municipal Health Bureau, recognizing the increasing number of births in the city, the high cost of childbirth, and the excessive burden on citizens, has added a maternal and infant health service to the health exchanges in the southern and northern districts of Shanghai. Experienced female doctors and midwives have been appointed to carry out the work, which has now begun to protect the safety of mothers, the health of infants, save on childbirth costs, and reduce the burden on citizens. The services include prenatal examination, prenatal visits, delivery, postpartum examination, and postpartum services. Provisional measures have been printed and are available for reading or telephone inquiries at any time. In addition, female doctors are responsible for handling gynecology, venereal diseases in women, pediatrics, and infant health examinations. If the public has any questions about maternal and infant health, they can go to the office at any time to ask everything, or call by telephone. The hours for the Shanghai South Health Office at the intersection of Fangxie Road and Xilin Road in the Nanshi are Monday, Wednesday and Friday from 9 am to 5 pm. The Shanghai North Office Qingyun Road in Zhabei is open Tuesday and Thursday from 9 am to 12 pm. For delivery and other matters, someone can be sent to invite or call and they can come immediately.

Rainfall Reduced This Year: Yangtze River Approaching Dryness

Shanghai-Hankou Water Level Lowest at Just Over Two Feet; Navigation Difficult, Shipping Companies All Complaining Bitterly

Although Shanghai yesterday recovered with drizzling rain, the rainy season is over, so the amount of rain poured is very small. Compared with last year, it is even less. At the same time, the climate is warm, and rice borers in the fields cannot be killed, causing great damage to crops. Details of each situation are recorded as follows:

Reduced Rainfall

A reporter learned from the Junchu Dredging Bureau that the amount of rainfall in Shanghai last month was only 1.85 inches. Compared with the rainfall of 3.2 [Number] inches in the same period last year, it decreased by more than 1.5 [Number] inches. Furthermore, in October of this year, Shanghai did not have any rainfall, so the climate this year is extremely dry. Therefore, infectious diseases in winter are also more numerous than last year. Recently, the weather has been warm, unlike winter, so rice borers in the fields cannot be killed and are easily bred. Therefore, crops will be damaged.

River Water Dry

At the same time, the amount of rainfall in the Yangtze River Basin this year is less than that of Shanghai. As a result, the water level along the river is falling daily and is approaching the trend of dryness. A reporter learned from the Jianghai Customs yesterday that the water levels along the coast from Wusong to Xuanxang are as follows: Yichang, the 14th, 2 feet 2 inches; Hankou, 2 feet 4 inches; Jiujiang, 4 feet 5 inches; Anqing, 3 feet 80 [Number] inches; Wuhu, 3 feet 6 inches; Zhenjiang, 6 feet 1 inch.

Difficult Navigation

The navigation draft limit is 12 feet 1 inch for the Wuhu to Jiujiang section downstream and only 9 feet 6 inches for the Jiujiang to Hankou section. As a result, medium-sized ships with slightly heavier drafts are also difficult to navigate. In particularly shallow areas, transportation is impossible without reducing the load and using barges. Although shipping companies have already increased shallow water fees, due to the early arrival of the shallow water season, operations are difficult, and business is declining. Everyone is complaining bitterly.

Invoices Indicating Unit Price of Goods Exempt from Penalties

The Dazhong Yaoji Knitting Factory and Hefeng National Goods Store in Dongjiadu, this city, were sent by stamp tax inspectors to the local court of this city for adjudications and fines of several yuan, because the invoices only listed the unit price of the goods and did not state the total amount. The Municipal Knitting Industry Association forwarded a request for an explanation. The Ministry of Finance's Tax No. 11462 replied that since the shipping invoice already contained the unit price of the goods, it could not be said that the amount was not stated. According to the Ministry of Finance's instructions, the Shanda Dazhong Yaoji Knitting Factory filed an appeal within the statutory period, and yesterday the original court amended its decision based on the Ministry's instructions and did not impose a penalty.

Public Concession Factory Accidents Last Month

According to news from the Public Works Bureau Information Office, 190 industrial and occupational accidents occurred in the Public Concession in November of this year. However, the number of lives lost as a result reached as many as 14. Nine women were injured. The causes of the accidents were generally clear in 172 cases. Investigation and instructions on preventive measures and aftercare were carried out in 106 cases. Analyzing the above-mentioned dangerous items by type of industry, 30 cases occurred in the textile industry, with 8 deaths, including the accident at the Gao Yongxing velvet factory on Arrabaster Road, which burned seven workers to death due to carelessness, which was truly a tragic event. There were two cases in the glass manufacturing industry, with two deaths, six cases in the housing construction industry, with one death, 42 cases in the machinery and hardware manufacturing industry, but no deaths, 28 cases in the transportation industry, with one death, six cases in the food and beverage manufacturing industry, with one death, and one case in the vehicle manufacturing industry, with one death. If we analyze it by cause, 59 cases were related to electrical machinery, with one death. Eleven people were burned, with seven deaths. Four people were injured by electric shock, with one death. Twenty-one people were injured by falling objects, with no deaths. Twenty-five people were injured by being crushed from a height, with two deaths. Ten people were injured by collisions, with one death.

Changshu Guild Hall Asks for Relief: Illegally Pledged Public Property

Dagon Society said that the public property of the Changshu Guild Hall in this city (previously reorganized from the Changzhao Rice Industry Guild Hall) was illegally pledged to the Pudong Bank and illegally auctioned. It was presented to the Municipal Party Department, Social Bureau, and Local Association President Du Yuesheng for relief. The original presentation reads: It is noted that our guild hall was established in the Guangxu period by merchants from Yumi Shipping. The money was collected to purchase land and build several houses at No. 31, Xinxin Street, outside Dadongmen. In the 21st year of the Republic of China, there was a dispute over property rights with merchants from Changshu inland. For the sake of determining ownership, Cao Zhenqing, former chairman of the Changshu Fellow Association, who has always been irrelevant to the guild hall, borrowed the name of the party department and deceived the ship merchants. He sent a letter to the custodian Zhang Chengxian and defrauded him of a land deed certificate. Xu Zaixiang came forward (it was found that the guild hall had no such person) and privately pledged it to Pudong Bank. After repeated negotiations, Cao Zhenqing claimed that it had been lost. When our guild hall reported to the Land Bureau to re-register, the bureau suddenly claimed that the land deed certificate had been taken care of by the Pudong Bank and could no longer be reported as lost. However, before accepting the pledge, Peabody Bank did not investigate with the guild hall whether the mortgage was with the guild hall's consent. This is illegal, one. According to the general practice of banks, all public property must be handled with care, and must never be accepted with private feelings or ignorance. According to government regulations, when public property is mortgaged and sold, it must be submitted to the competent authority for approval. Moreover, the land deed certificate was illegally pledged. This is illegal, two. The industry established by the funding of many people belongs to public property, while that established by the sole investment of individuals belongs to private property. Banks are not ignorant children, and do not understand human affairs. Now the bank forcibly recognizes the public property that has considerable relationship in history as Xu Zaixiang's private property and calls a deer a horse. The malpractices in this are confusing. This is illegal, three. In short, if this public property is mortgaged due to the economic difficulties of the organization itself, it deserves the crime. Even if it is auctioned, we will be willing to do so. Now it is bankrupt due to illegal pledging, so the accumulated sweat and blood of hundreds of ship merchants, the industry created by hardship, is ruined. People are ruthless, and ship merchants will inevitably feel regret and heartache. I respectfully think that you (Society) (Bureau) (President) (are the superior authorities for guiding and supervising people's organizations) (are local leaders). Please note that our guild hall has been difficult to build up, and grant relief at this time when it is about to be implicated and bankrupt. On the one hand, our guild hall will continue to appeal according to law, and look forward to the truth coming out and our property being returned. And we respectfully inform the wise people of the society not to easily take over and accept it before the property dispute is resolved. If it becomes a reality, our ship merchants will deal with it. I am about to present it in tears, and I cannot fully express my desire. Respectfully presented, the entire four hundred ship merchants of the Changshu Guild Hall in Shanghai kowtow together.
