Special Feature

Impressions of the Shanghai Support Suiyuan Movement

— Yafei

The citizens of Shanghai have always been very enthusiastic in supporting and assisting in the self-defense of the survival of the nation and its people; this has been fully demonstrated in the Shanghai January 28th Resistance War and the Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army. At present, although foreign aggression is becoming more rampant, the patriotic sentiments of the people are becoming more and more intense. Just look at the recent Suiyuan alarm, the brave resistance of our frontline soldiers, and the enthusiastic assistance of the people in the rear, and you can get a powerful lesson!

Suiyuan is our most forward line of national defense, and at the same time, it is our last line of national defense; because if this line of defense is destroyed by the enemy, our country will no longer be able to protect itself. However, our determination to resist must start from this line of defense, because it is the last barrier in the Central Plains of our country after the fall of the four northeastern provinces and the occurrence of the Hebei-Chahar incident. This Suiyuan war, which is related to the final survival of the country, was finally unveiled by the multi-faceted military and opened the prelude to the war; and the exciting and bloody news, from the cold northwest wind, from the newspapers everywhere, came that the temple was recaptured, the bandit pseudo-counterattack failed, the bandit army revolted, the enemy bombed Wulanhua, and the climate in the frontier dropped to thirty-seven degrees below zero... and the patriotism and enthusiasm of the soldiers guarding the frontier to defend the territory were even stronger than in the past anti-Japanese situation. Therefore, since the war preparation was launched, the Suiyuan support movement and the comforting of the soldiers in North China and other places have risen like wind and clouds, and the response has been enthusiastic.

What is especially gratifying and exciting is that we read many moving news in the newspapers every day, such as: prisoners in various prisons going on hunger strikes to help with donations, peddlers and rickshaw pullers and beggars saving food and selling it to dedicate to the country, children saving their candy and toy money to support Suiyuan, and various groups and manufacturers in this city launching one-day movements, one-corner movements, one-yuan movements, and even one-article (manuscript fee) movements. The women's community is also publicizing donations and donating woolen shirts, cotton clothes, gloves, earmuffs, etc.... These, these, are all prevailing for a while. So far, just take the Suiyuan support donations in Shanghai, the total number has been more than one million, which shows the unprecedented enthusiastic mood, showing the true spirit of national self-salvation.

Every day, the newspaper tells us about the good news from the front line, and also reports to us the donation situation and the amount of donations from many groups, manufacturers, and institutions; in those donations, there are stingy coins from the pockets of the rich, sweat and blood money from peddlers, rickshaw pullers, and workers, and powder money from ladies and misses. The large numbers are thousands or tens of thousands, and the small numbers are a few cents. Moreover, these days, wherever you go, you can hear a series of conversations about the situation in Suiyuan and the Suiyuan support donations. This Suiyuan support movement can be said to be a general mobilization of men, women, old and young throughout the country. Although no slogans have been posted and no slogans have been shouted, the deep impression that can never be extinguished can be obtained in the agitated emotions of every people and in the excited conversations of every citizen!

Local Customs and Anecdotes

Memories of Guangxi

— Fantongshan

The motive for going south to inspect commerce was a year ago, because the two provinces of Guangdong and Guangxi have worked hard in construction in recent years and have achieved excellent results. The establishment of factories and industries has been increasing day by day, which has been praised by the people of the country, and the richness of the deposits is enough to provide economic researchers with excellent market data. This summer, my friend Mr. Deng Shixiong had a proposal to go to these two provinces for field investigation, so I partnered with him to travel together, agreed to take the Xingbu route to Annam and then to Hanoi, and then from Zhennanguan to Longzhou, passing through Liuzhou and Wuzhou to Guangdong Province. For a long-distance inspection, but due to time constraints, we delayed for two weeks in Xingbu, Annam, etc., and then went to Zhennanguan from Hanoi, took the Longzhou route to Yong, and took a car from Longzhou to Nanning, which took no more than four sentences and arrived at the destination. We arrived there on July 8th, when the province was in the period of resisting × and saving the country. The ground of Nanning changed into the most important area, the military deployment was tense, and those who came and went to the area were inspected. When we first arrived there, we were excited to hear the cry of resisting × and saving the country.

I remember one of the most bizarre things was that there were rickshaws in the Nanning market (Wuzhou has rickshaws but no public buses), but only public buses. When asked why, it was said to be Li Bai's policies, that is, humanitarianism and egalitarianism, so rickshaws were not allowed to be set up. Public buses are available on all roads, and it is very convenient to get in and out, and it is stipulated that a bus must pass each station within every ten minutes, so that passengers do not have to wait for a long time. At the same time, soldiers have separate military public buses, which are also scheduled to travel back and forth, with stations on each road. There is no fare for riding this bus, which is funded by the central government, so there are no soldiers coming and going in the civilian public buses, but the fares are also very cheap, much more economical than Shanghai.

The folk customs of Nanning are very simple and also pay attention to etiquette. The transactions in the shops are also very polite. The people, whether old or young, have to undergo military training and have a very brave spirit. The whole province is uniformly "armed". During the period of military alert, they can immediately be formed into militias. When the military emergency is lifted, they will immediately be demobilized and return to their old business. This is in accordance with Sun Yat-sen's legacy of turning soldiers into farmers, which is the three-self policy implemented by Bai Jian Sheng. As for the women, they also receive military training and are very simple. Most of them wear cloth clothes and rarely patronize cosmetics. The women who come out are all in their original faces, showing a natural beauty, without rouge and powder and that kind of enchanting weirdness. This is a new record for the women's world in China. Recently, many women have participated in the organized militias. Their work is mostly in rescue teams, and there are also many others, such as service to the political and cadre work of the military divisions and brigades. In summary, the spirit of the people can reach this level because of the ruling spirit of their rulers, which is the result of the people's support and obedience.

Since Guangxi implemented the new policy, it has erected the four major districts in the province, namely Wuzhou as the commercial office, Nanning as the political district, Liuzhou as the industrial district, and Guilin as the cultural district. When we arrived in Liuzhou, it was another new scene.

Wuzhou is the text center of commerce, the streets are prosperous, the architecture is magnificent, surrounded by mountains, and the streets are mostly built on mountain slopes. The river runs through, and the scenery is very beautiful. There is a provincial tung oil factory, a pharmaceutical factory, a tap water factory, and a sulphuric acid plant jointly run by Guangdong and Guangxi. We visited the whole city and various factories. The tung oil factory is more developed, and the pharmaceutical factory is divided into two departments: chemical and pharmaceutical. It was opened in January last year, and the order is well-organized and very spirited.

Guilin is surrounded by mountains, and along the Li River, there are many clear streams and dangerous ravines, which are eye-catching and never tire of seeing. The so-called Guilin landscape is the best in the world, which is not a false statement. We only had a few days in Guilin due to time constraints. Visiting the famous scenic spots and historical sites is like riding a horse to watch flowers. We only get a rough idea. Later, we visited several secondary schools, which were very strictly managed. The results are needless to say, of course very good. The students there all wear gray cloth military uniforms and walk with a heroic spirit. They all have a martial spirit and have been fully trained, symbolizing that they are the pillars of the new China and the pillars of the rejuvenation of the nation.

The administrative facilities in Guangxi are completely based on the "Guangxi Construction Program" passed by the joint meeting of the Party, government, and army last year. The Guangxi Construction Program has a total of twenty-seven articles, divided into four major principles: politics, economy, culture, and military. They are all practical guides, not empty propaganda. Speaking of their political construction, they have now improved the political grassroots, promoted various construction undertakings, and vigorously implemented and promoted a political style of fairness, integrity, and incorruptibility, improved administrative transportation, and implemented civil servant training. All of the above are evidenced by facts and there have been considerable political achievements that can be proven.

Shanghai Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

The Xi'an Incident and Aid to Suiyuan

— Shi Yi

While the battle in Suiyuan has only come to a temporary halt, and the enemy is preparing to force his puppets to stage a comeback, unfortunately, we have witnessed the extraordinary Xi'an Incident.

Regarding the handling of the Xi'an Incident, the National Government's decree on the 13th clearly stated to us: "The government has its own appropriate handling of this Xi'an Incident. All government affairs of all institutions inside and outside the capital will continue as usual according to the established policy. The people of the whole country should also live in peace and industry, and must not lightly believe rumors and disturb each other..." Naturally, we do not need to "disturb each other." But we cannot deny the impact caused by the Xi'an Incident, or the blow the Xi'an Incident has given to the soldiers at the front and the people in the rear.

Due to the occurrence of the Xi'an Incident, we can see in today's newspapers that several Suiyuan support groups have urgently issued statements deciding to "postpone the assembly." Although the urgent convocation does not immediately produce the strength to support Suiyuan, it is a fact that the strength to support Suiyuan has also been "postponed" due to the "postponement."

On the other hand, due to the domestic incident, the enemy will seize the opportunity to attack, which will also become an inevitable fact; on the one hand, we have reduced the strength of Suiyuan support, and on the other hand, we have intensified the enemy's pressure. May I ask, how will this situation develop?

If the enemy invades, the soldiers of Suiyuan will fight more bravely against the enemy, which we firmly believe. The Xi'an Incident has been dealt with "appropriately" by the officials of the National Government, and turning hostility into friendship is what we desire and believe. Therefore, although the occurrence of the Xi'an Incident may make our emotions momentarily confused, after rational consideration, we should work more steadfastly because of the occurrence of the Xi'an Incident. Being confused and shocked by the incident will not only not help to resolve the incident, but will also make the incident more chaotic.

Based on the above understanding, I dare to offer sincere advice to compatriots across the country: we must not be so frightened all day long because of the extraordinary domestic incident that we neglect to resist foreign enemies. On the contrary, precisely because of the coming of the incident, which will induce greater pressure from foreign enemies, we should concentrate our efforts to actively fight and fight for the survival of the endangered motherland!

Therefore, the Suiyuan support movement, if not absolutely necessary, we should not only not postpone the assembly, but also "advance the assembly"; we should not only support Suiyuan as usual, but also do our best to support Suiyuan!

We should use facts to proclaim to all countries: The Chinese people, even in the midst of extraordinary domestic incidents, still have the power to resist foreign aggression!

Jinsha River

— Hangu

The people who live alongside the Jinsha River are accustomed to the scenery of the river.

The dawn devours the darkness, and the crowing of chickens lingers on the treetops along the riverbank. The river is covered with a thin layer of mist, which weaves into a hazy net in the distance, blurring together with the distant mountains. The radiant morning glow paints the horizon, like pieces of tattered bright red carpets, like piles of delicate and enchanting peach petals, piercing through the white mist, reflecting on the mirror-like river water, imprinting pale red floating clouds, and swaying mountains, lush forests, and nodding willows on the banks. On the road along the river and in the forests, one or two whistles from horse herders and the clanging of donkey and mule bells are heard from time to time. In the mountain forests, woodcutters sing mountain songs, floating with innocent laughter. Gradually, the smoke from cooking by the riverside rises in wisps, and the sunlight gently kisses the river surface, making the Jinsha River more brilliant. It seems as if a peach blossom forest is blooming at the bottom of the water.

On moonlit nights, the Jinsha River becomes thinner. The white moonlight reflects on the white water, and the river surface is vast, like a ten-mile plain. A gentle breeze stirs up ripples on the water, and wave-like patterns rise and fall in layers, like wheat waves. The mountains and forests at the bottom of the river sway like cradles. The barking of dogs in the riverside village, mixed with the howling of wolves on the mountain, echoes back from the high ground, making the moonlight and the Jinsha River even more desolate. Fishermen light torches, hold nets, wait for the fish baskets to fill with live fish, and return singing mountain songs. They will sell the fish tomorrow morning, buy a couple of catties of liquor, and drink until they are dazed.

When the autumn wind blows on the river surface, the Jinsha River puts on a turquoise jacket, and the sky printed at the bottom of the water is indistinguishable in color from the river water. The red trees on the mountain set off the green river water, making it more vibrant. The withered yellow willow leaves are blown into the river by the wind, drifting with the waves, and the large stones by the river gradually emerge. The water becomes clearer and shallower day by day. The women of the riverside village sit on large stones washing clothes until the sun inclines to the west before carrying their large bundles on their backs and returning in the setting sun, accompanied by the songs of the cowherds on the mountain.

If it is the season when willow catkins drift, the Jinsha River is plumper. Wildflowers dot the quietly standing mountains. Some unknown insects quietly crawl over the grass. Thrushes and turtle doves hop and jump in the forest, singing various tunes joyfully and loudly. Flocks of sheep leisurely stroll through the willow forests by the flower river, singing sad songs, innocently intoxicated by the flower-green nature, rendering the scenery on the river even more intoxicating.

The cuckoo bird cries out the heat in the forest, and the Jinsha River pants, like a pregnant woman about to give birth. Dark clouds gallop in the sky, a flash of lightning sweeps across the river surface, and a crack of thunder bursts, and heavy rain pours into the river. Then, the river, the mountains, and the valleys become a vast expanse of whiteness. But as soon as the sun comes out, the river changes its appearance again.

Visiting the Shanghai Fish Farming Industrial School

— Fang Zhou

Yesterday, I went to Dachang to visit the Shanghai Fish Farming Industrial School.

We got off the bus at Yuqing Bridge, asked many times, and finally found Yangshu Garden. As usual, we explained our intentions to the owner of the garden, and he sent someone to open the gate of the fish farm and guide us to visit.

The fish farm is opposite the garden, covering an area of about two mu. There is also a garden next to it, but it is still under planning and construction. The location of the fish pond was originally a branch of a small river. After they made some modifications and built a dam at one end to isolate it from the river, it became a long fish pond. The pond is not very deep. The deepest part of the water is no more than two zhang, and now it is only one zhang or so. There are currently five types of fish fry in the pond: white fish, grass carp, silver carp, common carp, and bighead carp. Among them, white fish are the most numerous, followed by grass carp. In terms of profit, bighead carp are the most profitable, and common carp are the least profitable, because bighead carp grow quickly and the feed is common. On average, they can be harvested and sold in eight months.

Currently, there are a total of 1,500 fish fry in their pond, and each fish is about four or five taels, but it is still in the trial period, and all the equipment is very simple.

The location is very good. There is no shortage or excess of water, because there is a river next to the pond, a bay of green water, and several drooping willows. In the season of bright spring or long hot summer, I believe this scenery must be very lovely.

After visiting the fish pond, we returned to Yangshu Garden. The garden covers an area of about three mu, surrounded by fences built with boards. In the middle stands a Western-style building and a low-lying worker's house. Half of it is a horticultural garden and chicken farm, and the other half is being dug to prepare for raising American precious giant frogs.

After visiting all the places, the garden owner invited us to the reception room. At the same time, he told us that he was from Guangdong, because he himself was very interested in studying rural sideline occupations, especially he felt that fish farming is a cause that is worth promoting in our country.

One mu of fish pond can raise about 2,000 to 4,000 fish.

Page 21

Each year, the fish is harvested once. The growth rate of the fish is that bighead carp can grow more than one catty per year, grass carp and white fish are about one catty, and common carp are only ten to eleven taels. The common feed is mostly aquatic plants and various soft-bodied animals. Each mu of pond costs about 100 to 200 yuan per year, and the harvest is also 200 to 400 yuan. According to this calculation, one mu of fish pond can yield about 100 to 200 yuan per year, and if ten mu of fish pond are managed, there can be a profit of 1,000 to 2,000 yuan per year.

Fish ponds in lakeside areas are at least five mu or more, but the most afraid of those who manage fish ponds are floods and the intrusion of black fish into the pond, because these are the disasters of fish farmers.

It is said that all the fish fry in their pond were transported from Suzhou and other places, but it is not necessary to put crucian carp species in any pond, and there will be crucian carp in the future, because the reason is that crucian carp can rush in from the water or bring fish roe from the aquatic plants, and hatch in the pond.

The motive for the title "Fish Farming Industrial School" is to plan to give all comrades who are interested in the fish industry practical opportunities in the future, but it is currently still in preparation.

Aftersound

Since the Shanghai Opera Company presented four issues of loose-leaf songs, "Spring Flower," "Brave Youth," "Your Lover is Him," and "Goodbye Friends," there have been many requests. The initial print of one thousand copies is about to be given away. A reprint is now imminent. Listeners who love songs can attach five cents to the Shanghai Opera Company, and a copy will be sent immediately.

Film

Nanjing Re-Releases "Chastity"

Since the Nanjing Grand Theater honorably presented MGM's blockbuster "Chastity" last week, the audience has been as high as the tide every day, so that many people are unable to get tickets. The reason why this film is so embraced by audiences around the world is really because of the touching story, the famous actors, the magnificent scenery, and the successful director. This time, the Nanjing Grand Theater, in response to the enthusiastic demands of all walks of life, will re-release "Chastity" for three days after "La Dame aux Camélias."

"Thunderstorm" Lead Actress Zhao Huaishen Comes to Shanghai to Film "Street Angel"

Ms. Zhao Huaishen, the mainstay of the China Traveling Theater Troupe and the younger sister of writer Zhao Jingshen, is well-known in the drama world. When the plays "Thunderstorm" and "Resurrection" were performed in Peiping, Shanghai, and the two Hubei provinces, they were famous far and wide. Ms. Zhao's portrayal of a cold, gloomy, and somewhat morbid character in these two plays is particularly profound. Recently, Yuan Muzhi's new work "Street Angel" by the Star Film Company has a prostitute role, which is a character who has experienced many vicissitudes and tasted the sweetness and bitterness of life. It is quite suitable for the character played by Ms. Huaishen. Therefore, Yuan Muzhi consulted with Mr. Tang Kuichou and temporarily borrowed Ms. Zhao from the China Traveling Theater Troupe. The agreement has been finalized, and Ms. Zhao Huaishen set off from Hunan to Shanghai yesterday. After resting for a few days, she will soon begin living under the mercury lamp.

A Collection of Interesting Facts About "Female Student"

Chen Qixia, the lead actress of "Female Student," went to Baidai Company yesterday to record the new songs "Female Student" and "Spring Breeze Niaona" from "Female Student," accompanied by the Baidai Orchestra. The chapters were sonorous, and the singing was graceful, with very satisfactory results.

There is an early exercise scene in "Female Student." A practical shooting was held at China Middle School the other day. The male students were trained by a military instructor, and the female students did freehand exercises, directed by Teacher Shen. The movements were neat and the spirit was lively. The lead actors of the film, Chen Qixia and Tao Jin, also joined the performance, full of vigor, which made people yearn for it.

Fan Xuepeng, who plays the blind old woman in "Female Student," and Liang Kaiyuan, who plays the blind old woman's young son, are an old pair of partners in "Mother." In "Female Student," the two play a mother and son who have suffered a lot, and their expressions are even more moving than in "Mother."

Leng Bo played a small rickshaw puller in "By the Huangpu River." Because he was careless in pushing the cart, he fell into the river from the bridge. Now, in "Female Student," he plays an old carpenter who also falls from the scaffolding because he lost his footing while building a house. He falls again and again, which can be described as a falling star shining brightly.
